WHEREAS                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(1) The Oil Fields (Regulation and Development) Act, 1948 (53 of 1948) (hereinafter referred to             <br /><br /><br />
as “the Act") and the Petroleum and Natural Gas Rules, 1959, made thereunder (hereinafter                   <br /><br /><br />
referred to as "the Rules") make provision inter-alia for the regulation of Petroleum                       <br /><br /><br />
Operations and the grant of licenses and leases for exploration and development of Petroleum                <br /><br /><br />
m India;                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿(2)    The Rules provide for the grant ojf exploration licences and mining leases in respect of land  <br /><br /><br />
vested in a State Government by that State Government 'with previous approval of the                  <br /><br /><br />
Central Government; and ONGC is bong granted petroleum exploration license to carry out               <br /><br /><br />
Exploration Operations in association with other Companies in that area onshore identified            <br /><br /><br />
as Block AA-ON/7 and more particularly described in Appendix A;                                       <br /><br /><br />
(3)    The Rules provide for an agreement between the Government and the Licensee with respect        <br /><br /><br />
to additional terms and conditions in regard to the license or lease;                                 <br /><br /><br />
(4)    The Government desires that the Petroleum resources which may exist in India be                <br /><br /><br />
discovered and exploited with the utmost expedition in the overall interest of India in               <br /><br /><br />
accordance with good petroleum industry practices;                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(5)    The Companies have represented that they have, or will acquire and make available, the         <br /><br /><br />
necessary financial and technical resources and the technical and industrial competence and           <br /><br /><br />
experience necessary for proper discharge and/or performance of all obligations required to           <br /><br /><br />
be performed under this Contract to provide guarantees as required in Article 29 for the due          <br /><br /><br />
performance of its undertakings hereunder,                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(6)    As a result of discussions between representatives of die Government and Companies on the      <br /><br /><br />
proposal of Companies, the Government has agreed to enter into tliis Contract with                    <br /><br /><br />
Companies with respect to the said area referred to in paragraph (2) above on the terms and           <br /><br /><br />
conditions herein set forth.-                                                                         <br /><br /><br />

contained, IT IS HEREBY AGREED between the Parties as follows;                                        <br /><br /><br />

 1.1    "Accounting Procedure" means the principles and procedures of accounting set out in                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 Appendix C.                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 1.2    "Affiliate" means a company that directly or indirectly controls or is controlled by a Party                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 to this Contract or a company which directly or indirectly controls or is controlled by a                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 company, wliich controls a Party to this contract, it being understood that "control" means                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 . ownership by one company or more than fifty percent (50%) of the voting securities of the                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 other company, or the power to direct, administer and dictate policies of the other                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 company even where the voting securities held by such company exercising such effective                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 control in that other company is less than fifty percent (50%) and the term "controlled"                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 shall have a corresponding meaning.                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 13    "Appendix" means an Appendix attached to tills Contract and made a part thereof.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 1.4    "Appraisal Program” means a program, approved by the Management Committee,                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 carried out following a Discovery of Petroleum in the Contract Area for the purpose of                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 delineating the Petroleum Reservoirs to which the Discovery relates in terms of thickness                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 and lateral extent and determining the characteristics thereof.and the quantity of                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 recoverable Petroleum therein.                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
1.5    "Appraisal Well” means a Well drilled pursuant to an approved Appraisal Program.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
1.6    "Arms Length Sales" means sales of Petroleum made freely in the open international                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
market, in freely convertible currencies, between willing and unrelated sellers and buyers                                                                <br /><br /><br />
and in which such buyers and sellers have no contractual or other relationship, directly or                                                               <br /><br /><br />
indirectly, or any common or joint interest as is reasonably and likely to influence selling                                                              <br /><br /><br />
prices and shall, inter-alia, exclude sales (whether direct or indirect, through brokers or                                                               <br /><br /><br />
otherwise) involving Affiliates, sales between entities comprising the Contractor, sales                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
between governments and government-owned entities, counter trades, restricted or                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
distress sales, sales involving barter arrangements and generally anytransactions motivated                                                               <br /><br /><br />
in whole or in part by considerations other than normal commercial practices,                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

﻿ 1.8    "Associated Natural Gas" or "ANG" means Natural gas occurring in association                                  <br /><br /><br />
 with Crude Oil either as free gas or in solution, if such Crude Oil cari by itself by                                <br /><br /><br />
 commercially produced.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 1.9    “Barrel" means a quantity or unit equal to 158.9074 litres (forty two (42) United States                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 gallons) liquid measure, at a temperature of sixty (60) degrees Fahrenheit (15.56 degrees                            <br /><br /><br />
 Centigrade) under one atmosphere of pressure (14.7 psia).                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 1.10    "Basement" means any igneous or metamorphic rock, or rock or any stratum of such                             <br /><br /><br />
 nature, in and below which the geological structure or physical characteristics of the rock                          <br /><br /><br />
 sequence do not have the properties necessary for the accumulation of Petroleum id                                   <br /><br /><br />
 commercial quantities and which reflects the maximum depth at which any such                                         <br /><br /><br />
 accumulation can be reasonably expected in accordance with the knowledge generally                                   <br /><br /><br />
 accepted in the international petroleum industry.                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 1.11    “Calendar Month” means any of the twelve months of the Calendar Year.                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 1.12 "Calendar Quarter" means a period of three consecutive Calendar Months commencing                               <br /><br /><br />
 on the first day of January, April, July and October of each Calendar Year.                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 1.13 “Calendar Year” means a period of twelve consecutive Months according to the                                    <br /><br /><br />
 Gregorian Calendar, commencing with the first day of January and ending with the thirty-                             <br /><br /><br />
 first day of December.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />

1.14 "Commercial Discovery" means a Discovery of petroleum reserves which, when produced, is                          <br /><br /><br />
likely to yield a reasonable profit on the funds invested in Petroleum Operations, after                              <br /><br /><br />
deduction of Contract Costs, and which has been declared a Commercial Discovery in                                    <br /><br /><br />
accordance with die provisions of Article 9 or Article 21, after consideration of all pertinent                       <br /><br /><br />
operating and financial data such as recoverable reserves, sustainable production levels,                             <br /><br /><br />
estimated development and production expenditures, prevailing prices and other relevant                               <br /><br /><br />
technical and economic factors according to generally accepted practices in the international                         <br /><br /><br />
petroleum industry.                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />

the Field and delivery of the same at the relevant Delivery Point under a program of                                  <br /><br /><br />
regular production and sale.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

﻿1.34 "Environmental Damage" means soil erosion, removal of vegetation, destruction of               <br /><br /><br />

shall include any damage or injury to, or destruction of soil or water in their physical            <br /><br /><br />
aspects together with vegetation associated therewith, aquatic or terrestrial mammals, fish,        <br /><br /><br />
avi-fauna or any plant or animal life whether in the sea or in any other water or on, in or         <br /><br /><br />
under land.-                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
1.35    "Exploration Costs" means those costs and expenditures incurred in carrying out             <br /><br /><br />
Exploration Operations, as classified and defined in Section 2 of the Accounting                    <br /><br /><br />
Procedure and allowed to be recovered in terms of Section 3 thereof.                                <br /><br /><br />
1.36    "Exploration Operations" means operations conducted in the Contract Area pursuant to        <br /><br /><br />
this Contract in searching for Petroleum and in the course of an Appraisal Program and              <br /><br /><br />
shall include but not be limited to aerial, geological, geophysical, geo-chemical,                  <br /><br /><br />
palaeontological, palynological, topographical and seismic surveys, analysis, studies and           <br /><br /><br />
their interpretation, investigations relating to the subsurface geology including structure         <br /><br /><br />
test drilling,’ stratigraphic test drilling, drilling of Exploration Wells and Appraisal Wells      <br /><br /><br />
and other related activities such as surveying, drill site preparation and all work necessarily     <br /><br /><br />
connected therewith that is conducted in connection with Petroleum exploration.                     <br /><br /><br />
1.37    "Exploration Period" mews a period not exceeding seven years commencing from                <br /><br /><br />
the Effective Date during which Exploration Operations may be carried out by the                    <br /><br /><br />
Contractor as provided in Article 2 hereof.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
1.38    "Exploration Well" means a Well drilled for the purpose of searching for                    <br /><br /><br />
undiscovered Petroleum accumulations on any geological entity (be it of structural,                 <br /><br /><br />
stratigraphic, facies or pressure nature) to at least a depth or stratigraphic level                <br /><br /><br />
specified in the Work Program.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
1.39    “Field” means an Oil Field or a Gas Field in respect of which Development Plan has been     <br /><br /><br />
duly approved in accordance with Article 9 hereof.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
1.40    "Financial Year" means the period from the first day of April to the thirty-first day of    <br /><br /><br />
March of the following Calendar Year.                                                               <br /><br /><br />
1.41    "Foreign Company" means a Company within the meaning of Section 591 of the                  <br /><br /><br />
Companies Act, 1956.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />

﻿                        ARTICLE - 2                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                         DURATION                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
2.1    The terms of this Contract, subject to the terras hereof and the applicable laws, shall          <br /><br /><br />
be for a period of twenty five (25) years from the Effective Date, unless the Contract                  <br /><br /><br />
is terminated earlier in accordance with its terms, but may be extended upon mutual                     <br /><br /><br />
agreement between the Parties for a further Period not exceeding five (5) years;                        <br /><br /><br />
provided that in the event of Commercial Production of Non Associated Natural Gas,                      <br /><br /><br />
the Contract may, by mutual agreement between the Parties, be extended for a period                     <br /><br /><br />
upto but not exceeding thirty five (35) years from the Effective Date.                                  <br /><br /><br />
2.2    The Exploration Period shall begin on the Effective Date and shall consist of three (3)          <br /><br /><br />
exploration phases for a total period not exceeding seven (7) consecutive Contract                      <br /><br /><br />
Years unless extended pursuant to the terms of this Contract.                                           <br /><br /><br />
2.3    Except as otherwise provided in this Contract, the term of the first exploration phase           <br /><br /><br />
shall be two(2) consecutive Contract Years (hereinafter referred to as Phase I),                        <br /><br /><br />
2.4    Except as otherwise provided in this Contract, the term of the second exploration                <br /><br /><br />
phase shall be three (3) consecutive Contract Years from the end of Phase I                             <br /><br /><br />
(hereinafter referred to as Phase II).                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
2.5    Except as otherwise provided in this Contract, the terms of the third exploration                <br /><br /><br />
phase shall be two (2) consecutive Contract Years from the end of Phase II                              <br /><br /><br />
(hereinafter referred to as Phase III).                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
2.6    At the expiry of any exploration phase of the Exploration Period, provided that the Contractor   <br /><br /><br />
has completed the minimum Work Program for that exploration phase, the Contractor shall                 <br /><br /><br />
have the option, exercisable by giving written notice to the Government at least thirty (30) days       <br /><br /><br />
prior to the expiry of the relevant phase, either:                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(a)    to terminate the Contract without obligation in respect of any subsequent phases                 <br /><br /><br />
of the Exploration Period; or                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(b)    . to proceed to the next exploration phase on presentation with the notice referred              <br /><br /><br />
to above of the relevant guarantee as provided for in Article 29; or                                    <br /><br /><br />
(c)    to relinquish the entire Contract Area except for any Discovery Area and any                     <br /><br /><br />
Development Area and to conduct Development Operations and Production Operations                        <br /><br /><br />
in relation to any Discovety in accordance with the terms of this Contract                              <br /><br /><br />
         If neither of the optlous provided for in paragraph (b) and (c) is exercised by the            <br /><br /><br />
     Contractor, this Contract shall terminate at thp end of the then current exploration phase.        <br /><br /><br />
C^AJ ILV) 1    -^2                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
﻿ 2.7  If, at the end of an exploration phase, drilling or testing operations are in progress on a     <br /><br /><br />
      Well not included in the minimum Work Program, such exploration phase shall be                  <br /><br /><br />
      extended for a period-not exceeding six (6) months provided that the minimum Work               <br /><br /><br />
      Program for such phase has been completed or the Licensee gives its consent to the said         <br /><br /><br />
      extension; and provided further that the period of such extension shall be subtracted from      <br /><br /><br />
      the period of the next succeeding exploration phase. In the event of an extension as            <br /><br /><br />
      provided for herein, the notice referred to in Article 2.6 shall be given at least thirty (30)  <br /><br /><br />
      days prior to the expiry of the relevant extension.                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
2.8    Where sufficient time is not available prior to the expiry of the Exploration Period to        <br /><br /><br />
complete the appraisal work on a Discovery, at the request of the Contractor, the                     <br /><br /><br />
Government shall extend the Exploration Period for such period, not exceeding thirty (30)             <br /><br /><br />
months as may be mutually determined by the Licensee and the Contractor, for the                      <br /><br /><br />
appraisal work to be carried out and for the Management Committee, the Licensee; and                  <br /><br /><br />
the Contractor to comply with the provisions of Article 9 and Article 21.                             <br /><br /><br />
2.9    If no Commercial Discovery has been made in the Contract Area by the end of the                <br /><br /><br />
Exploration Period, the Contract shall terminate.                                                     <br /><br /><br />

                                                         ARTICLE - 3                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                        RELINQUISHMENT                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
3.1    At the end of Phase I of the Exploration Period, in the event that the Contractor elects,      <br /><br /><br />
pursuant to Article 2.6, to continue Exploration Operations in the Contract Area in Phase             <br /><br /><br />
IJ, the Contractor shall retain seventy five percent (75%) of the original Contract Area              <br /><br /><br />
including any Development Area and Discovery Area in not more than three (3) areas of                 <br /><br /><br />
simple geometrical shapes and relinquish the balance of the Contract Area prior to the                <br /><br /><br />
commencement of Phase II.                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
3.2    At the end of Phase II of the Exploration Period, in the event that the Contractor elects,     <br /><br /><br />
pursuant to Article 2.6, to continue Exploration Operations in the Contract Area in Phase             <br /><br /><br />
HI, the Contractor shall retain twenty five percent (25%) of the original Contract Area,              <br /><br /><br />
including any Development Area and Discovery Area in not more than three (3) areas of                 <br /><br /><br />
simple geometrical shapes and relinquish the balance of the Contract Area prior to the                <br /><br /><br />
commencement of Phase III.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
3.3    At the end of Phase FH of the Exploration Period, the Contractor shall retain only             <br /><br /><br />
Development Areas and Discovery Areas.                                                                <br /><br /><br />
3.4    If the Contractor exercises the option provided for in paragraph (c) of Article 2.6, the       <br /><br /><br />
Contractor shall, after any Field and Development Area have been designated, relinquish               <br /><br /><br />
all of the Contract Area not included within the said Field and Development Area.                     <br /><br /><br />
3.5    As and when the Contract is terminated under the provisions of Article 2 or in '               <br /><br /><br />
accordance with any other provisions of this Contract, the entire Contract Area                       <br /><br /><br />
remaining with the Contractor shall be deemed to have been relinquished by the                        <br /><br /><br />
Contractors as on the date on which the Contract is terminated.                                       <br /><br /><br />
3.6    Relinquishment of all or part of the Contract Areas or termination of the Contract             <br /><br /><br />
shall not be construed as absolving the Contractor of any liability undertaken or                     <br /><br /><br />
incurred by the Contractor in respect of the Contract Area prior to the date of such                  <br /><br /><br />
relinquishment or termination.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
3*7 Any liability of the Contractor shall be limited to causes of action arising out conduct          <br /><br /><br />
of Petroleum Operations during the period between the Effective Date and date of                      <br /><br /><br />
said relinquishment or termination as the case may be.                                                <br /><br /><br />

Program specified for the relevant phase, is equal to the amount which will be required                           <br /><br /><br />
to complete the said minimum Work Program, in accordance with sound international                                 <br /><br /><br />
petroleum industry practices, reduced by the amount of the bank guarantee referred to                             <br /><br /><br />
in Article 29.1 (a).                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />

completed earlier than eighteen months from the end of the phase, the Contractor shall                            <br /><br /><br />

Contractor undertakes further work, subject to approval of the Management                                         <br /><br /><br />
Committee.                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />

shall be set off against the minimum Work Program for the following exploration                                   <br /><br /><br />
phase.                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />

﻿ ARTICLE - 5                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 MANAGEMENT COMMITTEE                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
For the purpose of proper performance of Petroleum Operations under the provisions of      <br /><br /><br />
this Contract, there shall be constituted a committee to be called the Management          <br /><br /><br />
Committee.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
The Management Committee shall consist of six (6) members, three (3) members               <br /><br /><br />
nominated by and representing Government and the Licensee taken together and three (3).    <br /><br /><br />
members nominated by and representing the Company(ies).                                    <br /><br /><br />
A representative of the Licensee shall be designated as the Chairman of the Management     <br /><br /><br />
Committee and a Deputy Chairman shall be designated from amongst the representatives       <br /><br /><br />
of the Government or the Licensee.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Parties may nominate alternate members with full authority to act in the absence and on    <br /><br /><br />
behalf of the members nominated under Article 5.2 and may, at any time, nominate           <br /><br /><br />
another member or alternate member to replace any member nominated earlier by notice       <br /><br /><br />
to other members of the Management Committee.                                              <br /><br /><br />
A quorum of the Management Committee shall consist of two (2) members representing         <br /><br /><br />
the Government and the Licensee and two (2) members representing the Companies.            <br /><br /><br />
The Management Committee shall review and have advisory functions in the following         <br /><br /><br />
matters:                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
(a)    the annual Work Program and budget proposed during the Exploration Period and       <br /><br /><br />
any revisions or modifications thereto submitted to it by the Operator through the         <br /><br /><br />
Operating Committee;                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(b)    proposals for surrender or relinquishment of any part of the Contract Area by the   <br /><br /><br />
Contractor;                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(c)    any other matter required by the terms of this Contract to be submitted to it for   <br /><br /><br />
review or advice;                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(d)    any other matter which the Contractor or the Operating Committee decides to         <br /><br /><br />
submit for review or advice including matters concerning inter-party relationships;        <br /><br /><br />
(e)    any other matter which the Management Committee desires to be submitted to it.      <br /><br /><br />
﻿    5.7 The following matters shall be submitted to the Management Committee for approval:         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
    (a)    annual Work Programs and budgets and any modifications or revisions thereto, as         <br /><br /><br />
    proposed by.the Operating Committee, for Development Operations and Production                 <br /><br /><br />
    Operations.                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
    (b)    proposals for an Appraisal Program, the declaration of a Discovery as a Commercial      <br /><br /><br />
    Discovery and the approval of Development Plans as may be required under this                  <br /><br /><br />
    Contract, or revisions or additions to an Appraisal Program or a Development Plan;             <br /><br /><br />
    (c)    delineation of a Field and a Development Area;                                          <br /><br /><br />
    (d)    appointment of auditors;                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
    (e)    collaboration with licensees or contractors of other areas;                             <br /><br /><br />
    (f)    claims or settlement of claims for or on behalf of or against the Contractor in excess  <br /><br /><br />
    of limits specified in the Operating Agreement or fixed by the Management                      <br /><br /><br />
    Committee from time to time, or as stipulated in the Contract;                                 <br /><br /><br />
    (g)    auy proposed mortgage, charge or encumbrance on Petroleum assets, Petroleum             <br /><br /><br />
    reserves or production of Petroleum;                                                           <br /><br /><br />
    (h)    any other matter required by the terms of this Contract to be submitted for the         <br /><br /><br />
    approval of the Management Committee;                                                          <br /><br /><br />
    (i)    any other matter which the Contractor or the Operating Committee decides to             <br /><br /><br />
    submit to it;                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
    (i) any other matter which the Management Committee decides should be submitted to             <br /><br /><br />
    it.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 5.8 'Hie Management Committee shall not take any decision without obtaining prior approval        <br /><br /><br />
      of the Government where such approval is required under this Contract or any applicable      <br /><br /><br />
      law (including rules and regulations) of India.                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
5.9 The Management Committee shall meet at least once every three (3) months or more               <br /><br /><br />
frequently at the request of any member. The Chairman shall convene each meeting by-               <br /><br /><br />
notifying the members at least twenty eight (28) days prior to such a meeting (or a shorter        <br /><br /><br />
period of notice if the members unanimously so agree) of the time and place of such                <br /><br /><br />
meeting and the purpose thereof and shall include in such notice a provisional agenda for          <br /><br /><br />
such meeting. The Chairman shall‘be responsible for processing the final agenda for such           <br /><br /><br />
meeting and the agenda shall include all items of business requested by the members to             <br /><br /><br />
be included, provided such requests are received by the Chairman at least ten (10) days            <br /><br /><br />
prior to the date fixed for the meeting, Matters not included in the agenda may be taken           <br /><br /><br />
up at the meeting by any member with the unanimous consent of all the members present              <br /><br /><br />
in the meeting.    ^    ^ _^gf                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
﻿5.10    The Chairman shall preside over the meetings of the Management Committee and, in his  <br /><br /><br />
absence, the Deputy Chairman or other member nominated by the Government or the               <br /><br /><br />
Licensee shall preside over the meetings.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
5.11 The Chairman shall appoint one of the members nominated by the Companies as Secretary    <br /><br /><br />
to the Management Committee with responsibility, inter-alia, for preparation of the           <br /><br /><br />
minutes of every meeting in the English language which shall be signed by each member         <br /><br /><br />
present at the meeting and provided to every member of the Management Committee with          <br /><br /><br />
two (2) copies of the minutes not later than twenty eight (28) days after the date of the     <br /><br /><br />
meeting.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
5.12    Within twenty one (21) days of the receipt of the minutes of a meeting, members shall <br /><br /><br />
notify the Chairman and the other members of their approyal of the minutes by putting         <br /><br /><br />
their signatures on one copy of the minutes and returning the same to the Chairman or         <br /><br /><br />
by indicating such approval to the Chairman by telex, cable, or facsimile, with copies to     <br /><br /><br />
the other members. Any member may suggest any modification, amendment or addition to          <br /><br /><br />
the minutes by telex, cable or facsimile to the Chairman and other members or by              <br /><br /><br />
indicating such suggestions when returning the copy of the minutes to the Chairman. If the    <br /><br /><br />
Chairman or any other member does not agree with the modification, amendment or               <br /><br /><br />
addition to* the minutes suggested by any member, the matter shall be brought to the          <br /><br /><br />
attention of the other members and resubmitted to the Management Committee at the next        <br /><br /><br />
meeting and the minutes shall stand approved as to all other matters. If a member fails to    <br /><br /><br />
appropriately respond within the aforesaid twenty one (21) day period as herein provided,     <br /><br /><br />
the minutes shall be deemed approved by such member.                                          <br /><br /><br />
5.13    The meetings of the Management Committee shall be held in New Delhi, India, unless    <br /><br /><br />
otherwise mutually agreed by the members of the Management Committee.                         <br /><br /><br />
5.14    All matters requiring the approval of the Management Committee shall be approved by a <br /><br /><br />
unanimous vote of ail the members of the Management Committee.                                <br /><br /><br />
5.15    A member of the Management Committee not present at a meeting may vote on any         <br /><br /><br />
matter on the agenda in such meeting by:                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(a)    appointing in writing, including by telex, cable or fax, another member of the         <br /><br /><br />
Management Committee as his proxy for that meeting; or                                        <br /><br /><br />
(b)    giving notice of such vote to the Chairman prior to the submission of such matter for  <br /><br /><br />
vote at such meeting.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
5.16    The Management Committee may appoint legal, financial or technical subcommittees      <br /><br /><br />
comprised of such representatives as may be agreed by the Management Committee to             <br /><br /><br />
consider any matter requiring approval ordecision of the Management Committee.                <br /><br /><br />

                    ARTICLE - 6                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 OPE RATORSHIF. OPERATING AGREEMENT .                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
              AND OPERATING COMMITTEE                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
6.1    Except as provided in Article 6.2 and subject to the terms of the Operating Agreement,         <br /><br /><br />
CENTURION shall be the Operator for the Exploration Operations, Development Operations                <br /><br /><br />
and Production Operations within the Contract Area during the term of the Contract.                   <br /><br /><br />
6.2    In respect of each Field in which the Licensee is participating, the Licensee shall have       <br /><br /><br />
the option to become the Operator of the Field at any time after ten years have                       <br /><br /><br />
elapsed from the date of commencement of Commercial Production from that Field.                       <br /><br /><br />
6.3    In the event the Licensee elects to exercise the option specified in Article 6.2, it shall     <br /><br /><br />
so notify the Contractor in writing atleast one hundred and eighty (180) days prior to                <br /><br /><br />
the date from which the Licensee would like to assume the operatorship and the                        <br /><br /><br />
transfer of operatorship shall be effected in accordance with the provisions of the                   <br /><br /><br />
Operating Agreement.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
6.4    Excepts as provided in Article 6.2, no change in operatorship shall be effected without        <br /><br /><br />
the consent of the Licensee and the Management Committee and such consent shall                       <br /><br /><br />
not be unreasonably withheld.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
6.5    The operating functions required of the Contractor under this Contract shall be                <br /><br /><br />
performed by the Operator on behalf of all constituents of the Contractor subject to,                 <br /><br /><br />
and in accordance with, the terms and provisions of the Contract and generally                        <br /><br /><br />
accepted international petroleum industry practice.                                                   <br /><br /><br />
6.6    Within thirty (30) days of the Effective Date, the Companies and the Licensee shall            <br /><br /><br />
execute a mutually agreed Operating Agreement. The said Agreement shall be consistent                 <br /><br /><br />
with the provisions of this Contract and shall provide for, among other things :                      <br /><br /><br />
(a)    the appointment, resignation, removal and responsibilities of the Operator;                    <br /><br /><br />
(b)    the establishment of an Operating Committee comprising of an agreed number of                  <br /><br /><br />
representatives of the Licensee and the Companies respectively, chaired by a                          <br /><br /><br />
representative of the Operator;                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(c)    functions of the said Operating Committee taking into account the provisions of the            <br /><br /><br />
Contract, procedures for decision making, frequency and place of meetings;                            <br /><br /><br />
(d)    Participating Interest, contribution to costs, default, disposal of Petroleum and              <br /><br /><br />
assignment as between the parties to the Operating Agreement.                                         <br /><br /><br />

                                             ‘ general rights and obligations                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                      OF THE PARTIES                            <br /><br /><br />

 7.1 Subject to the provisions of this Contract, the Contractor shaJI have the following        <br /><br /><br />
                            rights:                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(a)    the exclusive right to carry out Petroleum Operations excluding the right for            <br /><br /><br />
exploration and exploitation of coal bed methane in the Contract Area and to                    <br /><br /><br />
recover costs and expenses as provided in this Contract;                                        <br /><br /><br />
(b)    the right to use, free of charge, such quantities of Petroleum produced from any         <br /><br /><br />
Field as'are reasonably required for conducting Petroleum Operations in the                     <br /><br /><br />
Contract Area in accordance with generally accepted practices in the                            <br /><br /><br />
international petroleum industry. The use of quantities of petroleum for the                    <br /><br /><br />
purpose of conducting Petroleum Operations in the Contract Area shall be                        <br /><br /><br />
subject to audit;                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(c)    the right to lay pipelines, build roads, construct bridges, ferries, aerodromes,         <br /><br /><br />
landing Fields, radio telephones and related communication and infrastructure                   <br /><br /><br />
facilities and exercise other ancillary rights as may be reasonably necessary for               <br /><br /><br />
the conduct of Petroleum Operations subject to such approvals as may be                         <br /><br /><br />
required and the applicable laws in force from time to time for the regulation and              <br /><br /><br />
control thereof,                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(d)    the right of full and free access to available relevant data and samples (including      <br /><br /><br />
but not limited to technical data such as seismic, well information, well                       <br /><br /><br />
completion reports, and any other data • in the possession or control of                        <br /><br /><br />
Government or ONGC of the Contract Area). Such access shall be at the                           <br /><br /><br />
material, copying and reproduction cost to the Contractor. .                                    <br /><br /><br />
7,2 The Government reserves the right to itself, or to grant to the Licensee or others the      <br /><br /><br />
right, to prospect for and mine minerals or substances other than Petroleum within the          <br /><br /><br />
Contract Area; provided, however, that if after the Effective Date, the Licensee or             <br /><br /><br />
others are issued rights, or the Government proceeds directly to prospect for and mine          <br /><br /><br />
in the Contract Area any minerals or substances other than Petroleum, the Contractor            <br /><br /><br />
shall use its best efforts to avoid obstruction to or interference with such operations         <br /><br /><br />
within the Contract Area and the third parties and/or Government, as the case may               <br /><br /><br />
be, shall use best efforts to ensure that operations carried out do not obstruct or             <br /><br /><br />
unduly interfere with Petroleum Operations in the Contract Area.                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿ The. Contractor shall:                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(a)    except as otherwise expressly provided in this Contract, conduct all Petroleum        <br /><br /><br />
.Operations at its sole risk, cost and expense and' provide all funds necessary for          <br /><br /><br />
the conduct of Petroleum Operations including funds for the purchase or lease of             <br /><br /><br />
equipment, materials or supplies required for Petroleum Operations as well as.               <br /><br /><br />
for making payments to employees, contractors and Sub contractors;                           <br /><br /><br />
(b)    conduct all Petroleum Operations within the Contract Area diligently,                 <br /><br /><br />
expeditiously, efficiently and in a safe and workman like manner in accordance               <br /><br /><br />
with good petroleum industry practice pursuant to the approved Work                          <br /><br /><br />
Programs;                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(c)    ensure provision of all information data, samples etc., which the Licensee may be     <br /><br /><br />
required to furnish under the applicable laws;                                               <br /><br /><br />
(d)    ensure that all equipment, materials, supplies, plant and installations used by the   <br /><br /><br />
Contractor, the Operator, and Subcontractors comply with generally accepted                  <br /><br /><br />
standards in the international petroleum industry and are of proper construction             <br /><br /><br />
. and kept; in good working order;                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(e)    in the preparation and implementation of work Programs and in the conduct of          <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations, follow good international petroleum industry practices                 <br /><br /><br />
with such degree of diligence and prudence reasonably and ordinarily exercised               <br /><br /><br />
by experienced parties engaged in a similar activity under similar circumstances             <br /><br /><br />
and conditions;                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(0 establish and submit to the Management Committee for approval appropriate                 <br /><br /><br />
criteria and procedures for the purchase, lease or rental of machinery,                      <br /><br /><br />
' equipment, assets and facilities required for Petroleum Operations based on                <br /><br /><br />
economic considerations and generally accepted practices in the petroleum                    <br /><br /><br />
industry with the objective of ensuring cost and operational efficiency in the               <br /><br /><br />
conduct of Petroleum Operations;                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(g)    establish and submit for the approval of the Management Committee appropriate         <br /><br /><br />
procedures including tender procedures for the acquisition of goods and services             <br /><br /><br />
as provided in Article 23.2;                                                                 <br /><br /><br />

﻿(i) appoint a technically competent and sufficiently experienced representative, and,       <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                           ARTICLE - 9                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                              DISCOVERY, DEVELOPMENT AND PRODUCTION                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 9.1 If and when a Discovery is made within the Contract Area, the Contractor shall:                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    forthwith inform the Government of such Discovery;                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    promptly thereafter, but in no event later than a period of tliirty (30) days from the                                               <br /><br /><br />
 date of such Discovery, furnish to the Government particulars, in writing, of such                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 Discovery;                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                  . (c) promptly run tests to determine whether the Discovery is of potential -commercial    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                  interest and, witlun a period of sixty (60) days after completion of such tests, submit a  <br /><br /><br />
                                                  report to the Management Committee containing data obtained from such tests and            <br /><br /><br />
                                                  its analysis and interpretation thereof together with a written notification to the        <br /><br /><br />
                                                  Government of whether, in the Contractor's opinion, such Discovery is of potential         <br /><br /><br />
                                                  commercial interest and merits appraisal.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
9.2    If the Operator determined to conduct a drill stem or production test, in open hole or                                                <br /><br /><br />
through perforated casing, with regard to any Discovery, it shall notify to the extent                                                       <br /><br /><br />
possible the Licensee of the time of such test at least twenty four (24) hours prior to                                                      <br /><br /><br />
the proposed test, and the Licensee shall have the right to have a representative                                                            <br /><br /><br />
present during such test.                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
9.3    If, pursuant to Article 9.1 (c), the Contractor notifies the Government, and the                                                      <br /><br /><br />

with a work Program and budget to carry out an adequate and effective appraisal of                                                           <br /><br /><br />
such Discovery designed to achieve both the following objectives: (i) determine                                                              <br /><br /><br />
without delay, and, in any event, within the period specified in Article 9.5, whether                                                        <br /><br /><br />
such Discovery is a Commercial Discovery and (ii) determine, with reasonable                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
precision, the boundaries of the area to be delineated as a Field.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
9.4    The proposed Appraisal Program shall be considered by the Management Committee                                                        <br /><br /><br />
within forty five (45) days after submission thereof pursuant to Article 9.3. The said                                                       <br /><br /><br />

the Yearly budget for the Exploration Period, adopted pursuant to Article 4, shall be                                                        <br /><br /><br />
revised accordingly                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

Article 9.6.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                   ARTICLE - 11                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                             MEASUREMENT OF PETROLEUM                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 11.1    The volume and quality of Petroleum produced and saved from a Field shall be measured                         <br /><br /><br />
 by methods and appliances generally accepted and customarily used in good international                               <br /><br /><br />
 petroleum industry practice and approved by the Management Committee.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 11.2    Net volume of Crude Oil and Natural Gas means Crude Oil and Natural Gas produced                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 from the well head minus the Crude Oil and Natural Gas used for Petroleum Operations                                  <br /><br /><br />
 and further exploration / exploitation or unavoidably lost or flared.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 11.3    The Government may, at all reasonable times, inspect and test the appliances used for                         <br /><br /><br />
 measuring the volume and determining the quality of Petroleum, provided that any such                                 <br /><br /><br />
 inspection or testing shall be carried out in such a manner so as not to unduly interfere                             <br /><br /><br />
 with Petroleum Operations.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 11.4    Before commencement of Production in a Held, the Parties shall mutually agree on :                            <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    methods to be employed to optimize the measurement of volumes of Crude Oil                                     <br /><br /><br />
 production;                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    the point at winch Petroleum shall be measured and the respective shares allocated                             <br /><br /><br />
 to the parties in accordance with the terms of this Contract;                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    the frequency of inspections and testing of measurement appliances and relevant                                <br /><br /><br />
 procedures relating thereto; and                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 (d)    the consequences of a determination of an error in measurement.                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 11.5 The Contractor shall undertake to measure the volume and-quality of the Petroleum                                <br /><br /><br />
 produced and saved from a Field at the agreed measurement point consistent with                                       <br /><br /><br />
 generally accepted practices in the international petroleum industry, with the frequency                              <br /><br /><br />
 and according to procedures agreed pursuant to Article 11.3. The Contractor shall not                                 <br /><br /><br />
 make any alteration in the agreed method or procedures for measurement or to any of the                               <br /><br /><br />
 approved appliances used for that purpose without the written consent of the Management                               <br /><br /><br />
 Committee and the Government.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
11.6                The Contractor shall give the Government timely notice of its intention to conduct                 <br /><br /><br />
                    measuring operations and the Government shall have the right to be present at and                  <br /><br /><br />
                    supervise, either directly or through authorized representatives, such operations.                 <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                          ARTICLE - 12                                           <br /><br /><br />
                       PROTECTION OF THE ENVIRONMENT                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 12.1 The Government and the Contractor recognize that Petroleum Operations will cause           <br /><br /><br />
 some impact on the environment in die Contract Area. Accordingly, in performance of             <br /><br /><br />
 the Contract, the Contractor shall conduct its Petroleum Operations with due regard             <br /><br /><br />
 to concerns with respect to protection of the environment and conservation of natural           <br /><br /><br />
 resources. Towards this end, and in the furtherance of any laws promulgated or as the           <br /><br /><br />
 Government may otherwise require from time to time, the Contractor shall:                       <br /><br /><br />
 a)    employ standard industry techniques, practices and methods of operation for the           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 prevention of Environmental Damage in conducting its Petroleum Operations;                      <br /><br /><br />
 b)    take necessary and adequate steps to:                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 (i)    preveot Environmental Damage and, where some adverse impact of the                       <br /><br /><br />
 environment is unavoidable, to minimize such damage and the consequential                       <br /><br /><br />
 effects thereof on property and people;                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 (ii)    ensure adequate compensation for injury to persons or damage to property                <br /><br /><br />
 caused by the effect of Petroleum -Operations.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
12.2    If the Contractor fails to comply with the provisions of paragraph (b)(i) of Article     <br /><br /><br />
12.1 or contravenes any relevant law, and such failure or contravention results in any           <br /><br /><br />
Environmental Damage, the Contractor shall forthwith take all necessary and                      <br /><br /><br />
reasonable measures to remedy the failure and the effects thereof.                               <br /><br /><br />
12.3    If the Government has, on reasonable grounds, good reason to believe that any works      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
or installations erected by the Contractor or any operations conducted by the                    <br /><br /><br />
Contractor are endangering or may endanger persons or any property of any person,-               <br /><br /><br />
or are causing or may cause pollution, or are harming or may harm wildlife or the                <br /><br /><br />
environment to a degree which the Government deems unacceptable, the Government                  <br /><br /><br />
may require the Contractor to take remedial measures within such reasonable period               <br /><br /><br />
as may be determined by the Government and to repair any damage to the                           <br /><br /><br />
environment. If the Government deems it necessary, it may also - require the                     <br /><br /><br />
Contractor to discontinue Petroleum Operations in whole or in part until the                     <br /><br /><br />
Contractor has taken such remedial measures or has repaired any damage caused.                   <br /><br /><br />
﻿12.4 The measures and methods to be used by the Contractor for the purpose of complying                 <br /><br /><br />
with the terms of paragraph (b)(i) of Article 12.1 shall be determined in timely                        <br /><br /><br />
consultation with the Government upon the commencement of Petroleum Operations                          <br /><br /><br />
or whenever there is a significant change in the scope or method of conducting                          <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations and shall take into account the international standards                            <br /><br /><br />
applicable in similar circumstances and the relevant environmental impact study                         <br /><br /><br />
carried out in accordance with Article 12.5 below.                                                      <br /><br /><br />
The Contractor shall notify the Government, in writing, of the measures and methods                     <br /><br /><br />
finally determined by the Contractor and shall cause such measures and methods to be                    <br /><br /><br />
reviewed from time to time in the light of prevailing circumstances.                                    <br /><br /><br />
12.5 The Contractor shall cause a person or persons with special knowledge on                           <br /><br /><br />
environmental matters, approved by the Government, to carry out an environmental                        <br /><br /><br />
impact studies in order                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(a)    to determine, at the time of the study, the prevailing situation relating to the                 <br /><br /><br />
environment, human beings and local communities, the wildlife and marine life in                        <br /><br /><br />
the Contract Area and in the adjoining or neighbouring areas; and                                       <br /><br /><br />
(b)    to establish the likely effect on the environment, human beings and local                        <br /><br /><br />
communities, the wildlife and marine life in the Contract Area and in the                               <br /><br /><br />
adjoining or neighbouring areas in consequence of Petroleum Operations to be                            <br /><br /><br />
conducted under this Contract and to submit, for consideration by the Parties,                          <br /><br /><br />
methods and measures contemplated in Article 12.4 for minimizing                                        <br /><br /><br />
Environmental Damage and carrying out Site Restoration activities.                                      <br /><br /><br />
L2.5.1 The first of the aforementioned studies if not covered under Article 12.5 shall be •             <br /><br /><br />
carried out in two parts, namely, a preliminary part wfucli must be concluded before                    <br /><br /><br />
commencement of any work in Contract Area relating to a selsmographic or other                          <br /><br /><br />
survey, and a final part relating to drilling in the Exploration Period. The part of the                <br /><br /><br />
study relating to drilling operations in the Exploration Period shall be approved by                    <br /><br /><br />
Government before the commencement of such drilling operations.                                         <br /><br /><br />
12.5.2    The second of the aforementioned studies shall be completed before                            <br /><br /><br />
commencement of Development Operations and shall be submitted by the                                    <br /><br /><br />
Contractor as part of the Development Plan, with specific approval of                                   <br /><br /><br />
Government being obtained before commencement of Development Operations.                                <br /><br /><br />

12.6 The Contractor shall ensure that:                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Petroleum Operations are conducted in an environmentally acceptable and safe                                        <br /><br /><br />
manner consistent with good international petroleum industry practice and that                                             <br /><br /><br />
such Petroleum Operations are properly monitored;                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(b)    the pertinent completed environmental impact study is made available to its                                         <br /><br /><br />
employees and to any person under its direct or indirect control and                                                       <br /><br /><br />
Subcontractors to develop adequate and proper awareness of the measures and                                                <br /><br /><br />
methods of environmental protection to be used in carrying out Petroleum                                                   <br /><br /><br />
Operations; and                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(e) the contracts entered into between the Contractor and its Subcontractors                                               <br /><br /><br />
relating to its Petroleum Operations shall include the provisions stipulated herein                                        <br /><br /><br />
and any established measures and methods for the implementation of the                                                     <br /><br /><br />
Contractor's obligations in relation to the environment under this Contract.                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
12.7 The Contractor shall, prior to conducting any drilling activities, prepare and submit                                 <br /><br /><br />
for review by the Government contingency plans for dealing with oil spills, fires,                                         <br /><br /><br />
accidents and emergencies, designed to achieve rapid and effective emergency                                               <br /><br /><br />
response. The plans referred to above shall be discussed with the Government and                                           <br /><br /><br />
concerns expressed shall be taken into account.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿12.7.1    In the evfent of an emergency,-accident, oil spill or fire arising from Petroleum                   <br /><br /><br />
. Operations affecting the environment, .the Contractor shall forthwith notify the                            <br /><br /><br />
Government and shall promptly implement the relevant contingency plan and                                     <br /><br /><br />
perform such Site Restoration Activities as may be necessary as provided, in                                  <br /><br /><br />
paragraph, (b) of Article 12.9.                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
12.7.2    In the event of any other emergency or accident arising from the Petroleum                          <br /><br /><br />
Operations affecting the environment, the Contractor shall take such action as                                <br /><br /><br />
may be prudent and necessary in accordance with good international petroleum                                  <br /><br /><br />
industry practice in such circumstances.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
12.8    In the event that the Contractor fails to comply with any of the terms contained in                   <br /><br /><br />
Article 12.7 within a period specified by the Government, the Government, after                               <br /><br /><br />
giving the Contractor reasonable notice in the circumstances, may take any action                             <br /><br /><br />
which may be necessary to ensure compliance with such terms and to recover from the                           <br /><br /><br />
Contractor, immediately after having taken such action, all costs and expenditures                            <br /><br /><br />
incurred in connection with such action together with such interest as may be                                 <br /><br /><br />
determined in accordance with Section 1.7 of Appendix C of this Contract.                                     <br /><br /><br />
12.9    On expiry or termination of this Contract or relinquishment of part of the Contract                   <br /><br /><br />
Area, the Contractor shall:                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
a)    subject to Article 27, remove all equipment and installations from the relinquished                     <br /><br /><br />
area or former Contract Area in a manner agreed with the Government pursuant to                               <br /><br /><br />
an abandonment plan; and                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
b)    perform all necessary Site Restoration activities in accordance with good                               <br /><br /><br />
international petroleum industry practice and take all other action necessary to •                            <br /><br /><br />
prevent hazards to human life or to the property of others or the environment with                            <br /><br /><br />
respect to Petroleum operations carried out by Contractor.                                                    <br /><br /><br />
12.10    In this Article, a reference to Government includes the State Government.                            <br /><br /><br />
12.11    If Contract Area is partly located on areas forming part of certain national parks,                  <br /><br /><br />
sanctuaries, mangroves, wetlands of national importance, biosphere reserves and other                         <br /><br /><br />
biologically sensitive areas, passage through the above mentioned areas shall generally                       <br /><br /><br />
not be permitted. However, if there is no passage, other than through these areas, to                         <br /><br /><br />
reach a particular point beyond these areas, permission of the concerned authorities                          <br /><br /><br />
shall be obtained.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />

said date.                                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

                                                                         ARTICLE - 14                                                           <br /><br /><br />
