                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 14.1 The Contractor shall be entitled to recover Contract Costs at the rate of one hundred                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 percent (100%) out of the total volumes of Petroleum produced and saved from each                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 . Field in the Year, separately for each Field, in accordance with the provisions of this                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 Article.                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 14.2 Exploration Costs incurred by the Contractor in the Contract Area upto the date of                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 Commercial Production of Petroleum from a Field in that Contract Area shall be aggregated,                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 and the Contractor shall be entitled to recover the aggregate of such Exploration Costs out of                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 the Cost Petroleum from the Field at the rate of one hundred percent (100%) per annum of                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 such Exploration Costs beginning from the date of such Commercial Production, as provided                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 in Article 14.4.                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
14.3    The Contractor shall be entitled to recover out of the Cost Petroleum from any Field in                                                 <br /><br /><br />
Contract Area, the Exploration Costs which it has incurred in that Contract Area in any                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Year after the Effective Date at the rate of one hundred percent (100%) per annum of                                                            <br /><br /><br />
such Exploration Costs beginning from the date such Exploration Costs are incurred as                                                           <br /><br /><br />
provided in Article 14A.                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
14.4    The Contractor shall be entitled to recover Exploration Costs as provided in Articles                                                   <br /><br /><br />
14.2 and 14.3 in proportion to the values of the quantity of Petroleum produced and                                                             <br /><br /><br />
saved from the Field as reduced by the Production Costs in the Field, in the relevant                                                           <br /><br /><br />
Year, provided that such Exploration Costs once recovered shall not be allowable for                                                            <br /><br /><br />
recovery second time.                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
14.5 Development Costs incurred by the Contractor in any Field upto the date of Commercial                                                      <br /><br /><br />
Production from such Field shall be aggregated, and the Contractor shall be entitled to                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
recover out of the Cost Petroleum from that Field the aggregate of such Development                                                             <br /><br /><br />
Costs at the rate of one hundred percent (100%) per annum of such Development Costs                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
beginning from the date of such Commercial Production from the said Field.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
14.6 The Contractor shall be entitled to recover out of the Cost Petroleum the Development'                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
Costs which it has incurred on such Field after the date of Commercial Production from                                                          <br /><br /><br />
the Field at the rate of one hundred percent (100%) per annum of such Development                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
Costs beginning from the date such Development Costs are incurred.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />

                                      incurred on a Field in that Year out of the Cost Petroleum from such Field.                               <br /><br /><br />

 Article 14.16:                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

 if such Costs were due for recovery in that Year, or the succeeding Years, until the                                    <br /><br /><br />
 unrecovered Costs have been fully recovered out of Cost Petroleum from the Field.                                       <br /><br /><br />

 Crude Oil.                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 accordance with Article 19) shall be aggregated with the value of Non Associated                                        <br /><br /><br />
 Natural Gas produced and saved from the said Field as though such revenues were                                         <br /><br /><br />
 realized from Non Associated Natural Gas.                                                                               <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                   ARTICLE - 16                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                            TAXES. ROYALTIES. RENTALS.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                               CUSTOMS DUTIES ETC.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
16.1    AJI Parties and the operations under the Contract shall be subject to all fiscal legislation in                            <br /><br /><br />
India except where, pursuant to any authority granted under any applicable law, they are                                           <br /><br /><br />
exempted wholly or partly from the application of the provisions of a particular law or as                                         <br /><br /><br />
otherwise provided herein.                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
16.2    Pursuant to the provisions of section 42 of the Income-Tax Act, 1961, the allowances                                       <br /><br /><br />
specified herein shall apply in computing income tax payable by a Company on its profits                                           <br /><br /><br />
and gains from the business of Petroleum Operations in lieu of (and not in addition to)                                            <br /><br /><br />
corresponding allowances provided for under the heading "Profits and Gains of Business                                             <br /><br /><br />
or Profession" in the Income-Tax Act 1961.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
16.2.1 Subject to the provisions herein below, deductions at the rate of one hundred                                               <br /><br /><br />
percent (100%) per annum shall be allowed for all expenditures incurred in respect                                                 <br /><br /><br />
of Exploration Operations and drilling operations. The expenditure incurred in                                                     <br /><br /><br />
respect of Development Operations, other than drilling operations, and Production                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Operations will be allowable as per the provisions of the Income Tax Act, 1961.                                                    <br /><br /><br />
The expenses so incurred are subject to the following :                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(a)    where any expenditure is not solely incurred on Petroleum Operations or is                                                  <br /><br /><br />
incurred as part of or in conjunction with any other busiuess, only that                                                           <br /><br /><br />
proportion of the total expenditure which can be proved to the assessing •                                                         <br /><br /><br />
officer to represent a fair proportionate part thereof, having regard to all                                                       <br /><br /><br />
relevant facts and circumstances, shall be allowed;                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Sections 40A and 44C of the Income-Tax Act, 1961, shall apply.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 16.2.2 Companies shall be entitled for income tax purposes only to deduct at the rate of                                          <br /><br /><br />
 one hundred percent (100%) of all of its unsuccessful exploration costs incurred in                                               <br /><br /><br />
 contract areas covered by other contracts from the aggregate value of Petroleum                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 allocable to the Contractor from the Contract Area:                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                     (a) Unsuccessful Exploration Costs incurred in contract areas other than the                                  <br /><br /><br />
                     Contract Area where Commercial Discovery has been made up to the date of                                      <br /><br /><br />
                     commencement of Commercial Production shall be aggregated and file                                            <br /><br /><br />
                     Companies) shall be entitled to deduct such costs at the rate of one                                          <br /><br /><br />
                     hundred per cent (100%) per annum;                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
﻿                  %                                   ARTICLE - 17                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                     CUSTOMS DUTIES                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
17.1    Machinery, plant, equipment, materials and supplies imported by Contractor or its              <br /><br /><br />
Subcontractors solely and exclusively for use in Petroleum Operations shall be exempted                <br /><br /><br />
from customs duties subject to compliance with procedures and conditions as may be                     <br /><br /><br />
determined pursuant to applicable customs duty legislation, Article 23 and the terms                   <br /><br /><br />
herein specified.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
17.2    Contractor shall submit to the Government a list of Subcontractors who are engaged by it       <br /><br /><br />
for the purpose of obtaining the various categories of items specified herein pursuant to              <br /><br /><br />
the conduct of Petroleum Operations and who may claim exemptions hereunder.                            <br /><br /><br />
17.3    In order to qualify for the exemption from customs duties as provided form Article 17.1,       <br /><br /><br />
all imported items for which duty exemption is being claimed shall be certified by a                   <br /><br /><br />
responsible representative of die Contractor to be imported in terms of this Contract solely           <br /><br /><br />
and exclusively for use in carrying out Petroleum Operations and shall be approved by a                <br /><br /><br />
representative of the Government to be eligible for such exemption pursuant to the terms               <br /><br /><br />
of the Contract.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
17.4 The Government shall have the right to inspect the records and documents of the physical          <br /><br /><br />
item, or items for which an .exemption is of has been provided under Article 17.1 to                   <br /><br /><br />
determine that such item or items are being or have been imported solely and exclusively               <br /><br /><br />
for the purpose for which die exemption was granted." The Government shall also be                     <br /><br /><br />
entitled to inspect such physical items wherever located to ensure that such items are being           <br /><br /><br />
used for the purpose herein specified and any item not being so used shall immediately                 <br /><br /><br />
become liable to payment of the applicable customs duties.                                             <br /><br /><br />
17.S Subject to Article 27, the Contractor and its Subcontractors may sell or otherwise transfer       <br /><br /><br />
 in India all imported items which are no longer required for Petroleum Operations, subject            <br /><br /><br />
 to applicable laws governh ------ ’    ' ' disposal of such items.                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿                           ARTICLE - 18                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
    DOMESTIC SUPPLY. SALE. DISPOSAL AND EXPORT                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                     OF CRUDE OIL & CONDENSATE                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 18.1    Until such time as the total availability to the Government and government Companies of                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 Crude Oil and Condensate from all Petroleum production activities in India meets the total                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 national demand as determined by the Government, each constituent of the Contractor                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 shall be required to sell to the Government or its nominee all of their entitlement to Crude                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 Oil and Condensate from each Field in order to assist in satisfying the national demand.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 18.2    Pursuant to. Article 18.1 and subject to Article 18.4, each constituent of the Contractor                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 shall offer to sell to the Government (or its nominee) its total Participating Interest share                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 of Crude Oil and Condensate to which it is entitled under Articles 14 and 15 at the price                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 determined in accordance with Article 19 for sales to Government and the Government                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 shall have the option to purchase the whole of the'crude at the said price.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 18.3    The aforementioned offer shall be made by a constituent of the Contract, in writing, at                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 least six (6) months preceding the Year in which the sale is to be made, specifying the                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 estimated quantities and grade of Crude Oil and Condensate being offered (based upon                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 estimates which shall be adjusted within ninety (90) days of the end of each Year on the                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 basis of actual quantities produced and saved). The Government shall exercise its said                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 option to purchase, in writing, not later than ninety days (90) prior to the commencement                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 of the Year in respect of wliich the sale is to be made, specifying the quantity and grade of.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 Crude Oil and Condensate which it elects to take in the ensuing Year. Failure by the                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 Government to give such notice within the period specified shall be conclusively deemed                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 an election to take all of the Crude Oil and Condensate offered (adjusted as provided                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 herein) in the ensuing Year.                                                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
18.4                                           I£ during any Year, India attains Self-sufficiency, the Government shall promptly                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                               thereafter, but in no event iater than the end of the first Calendar Quarter of the following                      <br /><br /><br />
                                               Year, so advise the each constituent of the Contractor by written notice. In such event, as                        <br /><br /><br />
                                               from the end of the second Calendar Quarter of the following Year, or such earlier date as                         <br /><br /><br />
                                               the Parties may mutually agree, Government shall have the option but not obliged to                                <br /><br /><br />
                                               purchase and the each constituent of the Contractor shall have the right to lift and export                        <br /><br /><br />
                                               its Participating Interest share of Crude Oil and Condensate until such time, if any as Self-                      <br /><br /><br />
                                               sufficiency shall have ceased to exist. If Self-sufficiency ceases to exist during a Year, the                     <br /><br /><br />
                                               Government shall recover its option to purchase under Article 18.2 in respect of the                               <br /><br /><br />
                                               following Year by giving notice thereof to the each constituent of the Contractor.                                 <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

 18.5 All payments in respect of sales to the Government pursuant to provisions of this Article                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                 shall be made by the Government within the period for credit applicable in the calculation                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                 of the price pursuant to Article 19. If no time frame for credit is applicable in such                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                 calculation, payment shall be made within forty five (45) days from the date of delivery of                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                 Crude Oil or Condensate to the Government at the Delivery Point. In the case of sales by                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                 a Foreign Company, payment shall be made in United States Dollars or any other                                            <br /><br /><br />
                           convertible currency acceptable to the Government and the Foreign Company, by wire                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                           transfer, to the credit of the Foreign Company’s designated account with a bank within or                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                           outside India designated by the Foreign Company. Subject to any change in the relevant                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                           laws, in the case of sales by a domestic company, payment shall be made in equivalent                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                           Indian rupees to the credit of the domestic company’s designated account with a bank in                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                           India designated by the domestic company. Notwithstanding the above, each constituent                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                           of the Contract shall submit an invoice to the Government within fifteen (15) days from                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                           the date of delivery of Crude Oil. All amounts unpaid by the Government by the due date                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                           shall, from the due date, bear interest calculated on a day to day basis at the LIBOR plus                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                           two percent (2%) will be paid.                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
18.6 If full payment is not received by a constituent of the Contractor when due as provided in                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
Article 18.4, it shall, at any time thereafter, notify the Government of the default and,                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
unless such default is remedied within fifteen (15) days from the date of the said notice,                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
such constituent shall have the right, unless otherwise agreed, upon written notice to the                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
Government;                                                                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                a) to suspend the sale to the Government purchase under Article 18.2;                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                b) to freely lift, sell and export all'its Participating Interest share of Crude Oil subject to                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                destination restrictions in accordance with Government policy, until the Government                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                has paid the due amount plus interest as provided herein;                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                c)                                                   if the payment plus interest is not received by each constituent of the Contractor                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     within one hundred and twenty (120) days from the date the said payment was due,                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     to receive and export the Government’s share of Profit Oil until such time as either                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     Government has paid all amounts due plus interest, or the value, based on the price                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     as determined in accordance with Article 19, of Government’s share of Profit Oil- so                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     exported is equal to all amounts due plus interest, whichever first occurs; provided,                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     however, that if the Government makes a payment to such constituent after it has                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     commenced export of Government’s share of Profit Oil and such payment together                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     with the value of Government’s share of Profit Oil exported (based on the price                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     determined in accordance with Article 19) exceeds the amount due plus interest,                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     necessary adjustment shall be carried out to refund to the Government forthwith the                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     excess the amount received by tbe constituent;                                                        <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
18.7    The Company shall be entitled to freely lift and sell / export any Crude Oil and Condensate                                                    <br /><br /><br />
which the Government has elected not to purchase pursuant to this Article 18, subject to                                                               <br /><br /><br />
Government's generally applicable destination restrictions to countries with which the                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
Government, for policy reasons, has severed or restricted trade.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
18.8    No later than sixty (60) days prior to the commencement of production in a Field, and                                                          <br /><br /><br />
thereafter no less than sixty (60) days before the commencement of each Year, the                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
Contractor shall cause to be prepared and submitted to the Parties a production forecast                                                               <br /><br /><br />
setting out the total quantity of Crude Oil that it estimates can be produced from a Field                                                             <br /><br /><br />
during the succeeding Year, based on a maximum efficient rate of recovery of Crude Oil                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
from that Contract Area (or those Contract Areas) in accordance with good petroleum                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
industry practice, no later than thirty (30) days prior to the commencement of each                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
Quarter, the Contractor shall advise its estimate of production for the succeeding Quarter                                                             <br /><br /><br />
and shall endeavor to produce the forecast quantity for each Quarter.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
18.9    Each Party comprising the Contractor shall, throughout the twin of this Contract, have the                                                     <br /><br /><br />
right to separately take in kind and dispose of all its share of Cost Petroleum and Profit                                                             <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum and shall have the obligation to lift the said Cost Petroleum and Profit                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum oh a current basis and in such quantities so as not to cause a restriction of                                                                <br /><br /><br />
production or inconvenience to the other Parties.                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
18.10    The Government shall, throughout the term of this Contract, have the right to separately                                                      <br /><br /><br />
take in kind and dispose of its share of Profit Petroleum and of such portion of the share                                                             <br /><br /><br />
of the constituents of the Contractor of Crude Oil as is purchased by the Government                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
pursuant to Article 18, and shall have the obligation to lift ail of the said Petroleum on a                                                           <br /><br /><br />
current basis and in such quantities so as not to cause a restriction of production or                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
inconvenience to the other Parties.                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
18.11 For the purpose of implementing the provisions of Articles 18.9 and 18.10, a Crude Oil                                                           <br /><br /><br />
lifting procedure shall be agreed upon by the Parties no later than six (6) months prior to                                                            <br /><br /><br />
the commencement of production in a Field. Such lifting procedure shall include, but not                                                               <br /><br /><br />
necessarily be limited to :                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 (a)                                          a procedure for notification by the Operator to the Government, and to each Party                        <br /><br /><br />
                                              comprising the Contractor, of projected Crude Oil production;                                            <br /><br /><br />
 (b)                                          a procedure for notification by the Government, and by each constituent of the                           <br /><br /><br />
                                              Contractor, to the Operator, of its expected offtake and the consequences of inability                   <br /><br /><br />
                                              or failure to offtake.    ^                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
﻿                        ARTICLE - 19                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                   VALUATION OF PETROLEUM                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
19.1    For the purpose of this Contract, the value of Crude Oil, Condensate and Natural Gas      <br /><br /><br />
shall be based on the price determined as provided herein.                                        <br /><br /><br />
19.2    A price for Crude Oil shall be determined for each Month or such other period as the      <br /><br /><br />
Parties may agree (hereinafter referred to as "the Delivery Period") in terms of United           <br /><br /><br />
States Dollars per Barrel, FOB Delivery Point for Crude Oil produced and sold or                  <br /><br /><br />
otherwise disposed of from each Contract Area, for each Delivery Period, in accordance            <br /><br /><br />
with the appropriate basis for that type of sale or disposal specified below.                     <br /><br /><br />
19.3    In the event that some or all of total sales of constituents of Contractor of Crude Oil   <br /><br /><br />
during a Delivery Period are made to third parties at Arms Length Sales, all sales so made        <br /><br /><br />
shall be valued at the weighted average of the prices actually received by the said               <br /><br /><br />
constituents, calculated by dividing the total receipts from all such sales FOB the Delivery      <br /><br /><br />
Point by the total number of Barrels of the Crude Oil sold in such sales.                         <br /><br /><br />
19.3.1    In the event that a portion of such third party Arms Length Sales are made on a basis   <br /><br /><br />
other than an FOB basis as herein specified, the said portion shall be valued at prices           <br /><br /><br />
equivalent to the prices FOB the Delivery Point for such sales determined by deducting all        <br /><br /><br />
costs (such as transportation, demurrage, loss of Crude Oil in transit and similar costs)         <br /><br /><br />
incurred downstream of the Delivery Point, and the prices so determined shall be deemed           <br /><br /><br />
to be the actual prices received for the purpose of calculation of the weighted average of        <br /><br /><br />
the prices for all third party Arms Length Sales for the Delivery Period.                         <br /><br /><br />
19.3.2    Each Company constituting the Contractor shall separately submit to the designated      <br /><br /><br />
nominee of the Government, within fifteen (15) days of the end of each Delivery Period,           <br /><br /><br />
a report containing the actual prices obtained in their respective Arms Length Sales to           <br /><br /><br />
third parties of any Crude Oil. Such reports shall distinguish between term sales and spot        <br /><br /><br />
sales and itemize volumes, customers, prices received and credit terms, and each                  <br /><br /><br />
constituent of the contractor shall allow the designated nominee of the Government to             <br /><br /><br />
examine the relevant sales contracts.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
19.4 In the event that some or all of the Parties’ comprising Contractor Company's total sales    <br /><br /><br />
of Crude Oil during a Delivery Period are made to the Government or its nominee, the              <br /><br /><br />
price of all sales so made shall, unless otherwise agreed between the Parties, be                 <br /><br /><br />
determined on the basis of either the FOB selling price per Barrel of one or more crude           <br /><br /><br />
Oils which, at the time of calculation, are being freely and actively traded in the               <br /><br /><br />
international market and                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
﻿ ?                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
are similar in characteristics and quality to the Crude Oil in respect of which the price is        <br /><br /><br />
being determined, such FOB selling price to be ascertained from Platt's Crude Oil Market            <br /><br /><br />
Wire daily publication (''Platt's''), or the spot market for the same crude oils ascertained in     <br /><br /><br />
the same manner, whichever price, in the opinion of the Parties, more truly reflects the            <br /><br /><br />
cunent value of such crude oils. For any Delivery Period in which sales take place, the             <br /><br /><br />
price shall be the arithmetic average price per Barrel determined by calculating the                <br /><br /><br />
average for such Delivery Period of the mean of the high and low FOB or spot prices for             <br /><br /><br />
each day of the Crude Oils selected for comparison adjusted for differences in the                  <br /><br /><br />
Crude Oil and the crude oils being compared for quality, transportation costs, delivery             <br /><br /><br />
rime, quantity, payment terms, the market area into wliich the crude oil is being sold,             <br /><br /><br />
other contract toms to the extent known and other relevant factors. In the event that               <br /><br /><br />
Platt's cases to be published or is not published for a period of thirty (30) consecutive           <br /><br /><br />
days, the Parties shall agree on an alternative daily publication. In the event of changing         <br /><br /><br />
market conditions, the Parties may review and mutually agree on changes to the period               <br /><br /><br />
over which the average price of comparable crude oils maybe calculated.                             <br /><br /><br />
19.4.1    At least six (6) months prior to commencement of production from the first Field          <br /><br /><br />
and from each Held thereafter in the Contract Area, the Parties shall meet in order                 <br /><br /><br />
to establish a provisional list of the crude oils to be selected for comparison with                <br /><br /><br />
the Crude Oil to be sold and an appropriate mechanism for the purpose of giving                     <br /><br /><br />
effect to Article 19.4 and definitively establishing the price of Crude Oil to be sold              <br /><br /><br />
pursuant to Article 19.4. In determining the quality of a Crude Oil, account shall                  <br /><br /><br />
be taken of all relevant characteristics including but not limited to gravity, sulphur              <br /><br /><br />
and metal content,, pour point and product yield.                                                   <br /><br /><br />
19.4.2    In the event that, at the relevant time, no crude oils of similar quality to the Crude    <br /><br /><br />
Oil to be sold are being actively traded in. the international markets where prices                 <br /><br /><br />
can be ascertained by international publication, or the official FOB selling prices                 <br /><br /><br />
and the international spot market price vary widely between producers, the Parties                  <br /><br /><br />
shall meet in good feith to determine an appropriate pricing basis.                                 <br /><br /><br />
19.4.3    The Parties shall meet annually, or sooner upon notice served by any Party on the         <br /><br /><br />
others, to review the list of selected crude oils or the mechanism established                      <br /><br /><br />

such crude oils or establishment of such mechanism and to determine what                            <br /><br /><br />
adjustment (if any) should be made to the said selection or mechanism by mutual                     <br /><br /><br />
agreement of the Parties.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                           ARTICLE - 20                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                  CURRENCY AND EXCHANGE CONTROL                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                            PROVISIONS                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 20.1 Subject to the provisions herein, and to compliance with the relevant provisions of the      <br /><br /><br />
 laws of general application in India governing currency and foreign exchange and related          <br /><br /><br />
 administrative instructions and procedures issued thereunder on a non-discriminatory              <br /><br /><br />
 basis, each Foreign Company comprising the Contractor shall, during the term of this              <br /><br /><br />
 Contract, have the right to:                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    repatriate abroad, in United States Dollars or any other freely convertible currency       <br /><br /><br />
 acceptable to the Government and the Foreign Company, the net proceeds of sales of                <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum in India;                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    receive, retain and use abroad the proceeds of any export sales of Petroleum under         <br /><br /><br />
 the Contract;                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    open, maintain and operate bank accounts with reputable banks, both inside and             <br /><br /><br />
 outside India, for the purpose of this Contract;                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 (d)    freely import, through normal banking channels, funds necessary for carrying out the       <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum Operations;                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 (e)    convert into foreign exchange and repatriate sums imported pursuant to (d) above in        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 excess (if any) of its requirements; and                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 (f)    make payments outside of India for purchases, services and loans obtained abroad           <br /><br /><br />
 without the requirement thatfunds used in making such payments must come from or                  <br /><br /><br />
 originate in India.                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 20.2 The rates of exchange for the purchase and sale of currency by the Companies shall be the    <br /><br /><br />
 rates in accordance with prevailing currency and exchange regulations and, for accounting         <br /><br /><br />
 purposes under this Contract, these rates shall apply as provided in Section 1.6 of               <br /><br /><br />
 Appendix "C".                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />

Government or any body designated by it, monthly bank statements with an explanation of            <br /><br /><br />
each deposit or payment from the account, and shall supply each quarter, in a form                 <br /><br /><br />
acceptable to foe Government, or such designated body, full particulars of foreign                 <br /><br /><br />
exchange, transactions pursuant to this Contract in order to facilitate monitoring of such         <br /><br /><br />
accounts. Such particulars shall indude:    ^                                                      <br /><br /><br />

      , sold, date of sale and unit price;                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
      (b)    the repayment of principal of loans made to the Contractor in foreign currency for       <br /><br /><br />
      purposes ofPetroleum Operations;                                                                <br /><br /><br />
      (c)    payments of interest, charges, fees and expenses in respect of loans referred to in      <br /><br /><br />
      paragraph (fa) above;                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
      (d)    payments in foreign currency to persons not resident in India for the supply of capital  <br /><br /><br />
      goods required for the purpose ofPetroleum bperations;                                          <br /><br /><br />

                                            ARTICLE - 21                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                             NATURAL GAS                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
21.1    Subject to Article 21.2, the Indian domestic market shall have the first call on the                        <br /><br /><br />
utilization of Natural Gas discovered and produced from any Field within the Contract                               <br /><br /><br />
Area. Accordingly, any proposal by the Contractor relating to Discovery and production                              <br /><br /><br />
of Natural Gas from a Field shall be made in the context of the Government’s guidelines                             <br /><br /><br />
issued from time to time for the utilization of Natural Gas shall take into account the                             <br /><br /><br />
objectives of the Government to develop its resources in the most efficient manner and to                           <br /><br /><br />
promote conservation measures.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
21.2    Contractor shall have the right to use Natural Gas produced from a Field for the purpose                    <br /><br /><br />
of Petroleum Operations including, but not limited to re-injection for pressure                                     <br /><br /><br />
maintenance, gas lifting ,and power generation etc.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
21.3    For tlie purpose of sales to the domestic market pursuant to this Article 21, the Contractor                <br /><br /><br />
shall have freedom to market the gas.                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
21.4    Associated Natural Gas (ANG)                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
21.4.1 In the event that a Discovery of Crude Oil contains ANG, Contractor shall declare                            <br /><br /><br />
in the proposal for the declaration of the said Discovery as a Commercial                                           <br /><br /><br />
Discovery as specified in Article 10, whether (and by what amount) the estimated                                    <br /><br /><br />
production of ANG is anticipated to exceed the quantities of ANG which will be                                      <br /><br /><br />
used in accordance with Article 21.2 (such excess being hereinafter referred to as                                  <br /><br /><br />
“the Excess ANG”). In such an event the Contractor shall indicate whether, on the                                   <br /><br /><br />
basis of the available data and information, it has reasonable grounds for believing                                <br /><br /><br />
tliat the Excess ANG could be commercially exploited in accordance with the                                         <br /><br /><br />
terms of this Contract alongwith the Commercial Production of the Crude Oil from. ’                                 <br /><br /><br />
the Oil Field, and whether the Contractor intends to so exploit the Excess ANG.                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 21.4.2 Based on the principle of full utilization and minimum flaring of ANG, a proposed                           <br /><br /><br />
 Development Plan for an Oil Field shall, to the extent practicable, include a plan                                 <br /><br /><br />
 for utilization of the ANG including estimated quantities to be flared, re-injected,                               <br /><br /><br />
 and to be used for Petroleum Operations; and, if the Contractor proposes to                                        <br /><br /><br />
 commercially exploit the Excess ANG for sale in the domestic market in                                             <br /><br /><br />
 accordance with Government’s guidelines, or elsewhere, the proposed plans for                                      <br /><br /><br />
                        such exploitation.    ,    -7                                                               <br /><br /><br />
﻿21.4.3    If the Contractor wishes to exploit the Excess ANG, subject to Article 21.1 the <br /><br /><br />
Contractor shall be free to explore markets for the commercial exploitation of the'       <br /><br /><br />
said Excess ANG and submit its proposals for such exploitation to the Government          <br /><br /><br />
in accordance with Article 21.4.2.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
21.4.4    Where the Contractor is of the view that Excess ANG cannot be commercially      <br /><br /><br />
exploited and chooses not to exploit the said Excess ANG, or is unable to find            <br /><br /><br />
a market for the Excess ANG pursuant to Article 21.4.3, the Government shall be           <br /><br /><br />
entitled to take and utilize such Excess ANG.                                             <br /><br /><br />
21.4.5    If the Government elects to take the Excess ANG as provided in Article 21.4.4 : <br /><br /><br />
a)    the Contractor shall deliver such Excess ANG to the Government (or its              <br /><br /><br />
nominee) free of cost, at the downstream flange of the gas/oil separation                 <br /><br /><br />
.facilities;                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
b)    the Contractor shall based on sound petroleum engineering practices, install        <br /><br /><br />
such facilities as would facilitate, in so far as practicable, uninterrupted delivery     <br /><br /><br />
of such Excess ANG to the Government or its nominee;                                      <br /><br /><br />
c)    the cost of all facilities installed pursuant to paragraph (b) above shall be       <br /><br /><br />
recoverable as Contract Costs;                                                            <br /><br /><br />
• d) the Government or its nominee shall bear all costs including gathering, treating,    <br /><br /><br />
processing and transporting costs beyond the downstream flange of the gas/oil             <br /><br /><br />
separation facilities; and                                                                <br /><br /><br />
e) the delivery of such Excess ANG shall be subject to procedures to be agreed            <br /><br /><br />
between the Government or its nominee and the Contractor prior to such .                  <br /><br /><br />
delivery, such procedures to include matters relating to timing of off-take of            <br /><br /><br />
such Excess ANG.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
21.4.6 Excess ANG which is not commercially exploited by the Contractor, or taken by      <br /><br /><br />
the Government or its nominee pursuant to this Article 21, shall be returned to the       <br /><br /><br />
subsurface structure or flared or otherwise disposed of as approved by the                <br /><br /><br />
Government in the context of the Development Plan, provided that flaring will be          <br /><br /><br />
resorted to only for small quantities and as a last resort, provided that Contractor      <br /><br /><br />
shall at all times be entitled to flare the Excess ANG which is not taken by any          <br /><br /><br />
consumer, private or Government Agency with whom there is a valid contract of             <br /><br /><br />
upliftment of ANG produced from the Contract Area.                                        <br /><br /><br />

 21.5.3 If the Management Committee, with the approval of the Government, declares the                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 Discovery a Commercial Discovery, contractor shall, within one (1) Calendar Year                      <br /><br /><br />
 of the declaration of the Discovery as a Commercial Discovery, submit a                               <br /><br /><br />
 Development Plan for the development of the Discovery to the Management                               <br /><br /><br />
 Committee and the Government for approval. Such Plan shall be supported by all                        <br /><br /><br />
 relevant information including, inter alia, the information required in Article 9.7.                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 21.5.9 The Management Committee shall consider the proposed Development Plan and                      <br /><br /><br />
 submit its recommendations to Government within one hundred and eighty-(180)                          <br /><br /><br />
 days of submission thereof by the Contractor. The Government shall respond to                         <br /><br /><br />
 the proposed Development Plan within ninety (90) days of receipt of the                               <br /><br /><br />
 recommendations from the Management Committee provided that the Government                            <br /><br /><br />
 shall not be bound by the recommendation or decision of the Management                                <br /><br /><br />
 Committee. If the Management Committee foils to submit its recommendations to.                        <br /><br /><br />
 Government within the said ninety (90) days period, the Government shall in any                       <br /><br /><br />
 event respond to the Contractor within 270 days from the date of submission of                        <br /><br /><br />
 the proposed Development Plan.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 21.5.10 If the Government has failed to approve or disapproves the Contractor’s proposed              <br /><br /><br />
 Development Plan, the Government shall advise the Contractor, in writing, of the                      <br /><br /><br />
 reasons for such failure or disapproval and the Government and the Contractor                         <br /><br /><br />
 shad meet to discuss the said Development Plan and the reasons for the said failure -                 <br /><br /><br />
 to approve or disapprove, and use their best efforts to agree on appropriate                          <br /><br /><br />
 modifications thereto to meet the Governments concerns or objections. Thereafter,                     <br /><br /><br />
 the Contractor shall have the right to resubmit, within ninety (90) days of                           <br /><br /><br />
 communication from the Government, the proposed Development Plan duly                                 <br /><br /><br />
 amended to meet the Governments concerns. Such right of re-submission of the                          <br /><br /><br />
 proposed Development Plan shall be exercisable by the Contractor only once. If no                     <br /><br /><br />
 such Plan is submitted to the Government within the above specified period, the                       <br /><br /><br />
 Contractor shall relinquish its rights to develop such Gas-Discovery and such                         <br /><br /><br />
 Discovery shall be excluded from the Contract Area.                                                   <br /><br /><br />

21,6 Valuation ofNatural Gas                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
21.6.1 The Contractor shall endeavor to sell all Natural Gas produced and saved from the                       <br /><br /><br />
Field at competitive fair market arms-length prices.                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 21.6.2 Notwithstanding Article 21.6.1, Natural Gas produced from the Contract Area                            <br /><br /><br />
 shall be valued for the purposes of this Contract as follows :                                                <br /><br /><br />
 a)    Gas which is flared with the approval of the Government or re-injected shall be                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 ascribed a zero value;                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 b)    Gas which is sold to the Government or any other Government nominee shall                               <br /><br /><br />
 be valued at the prices actually obtained; and                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 c)    Gas which is sold or disposed of otherwise than in accordance with paragraph                            <br /><br /><br />
 (a) or (b) shall be valued on the basis of competitive Anns Length Sales in the                               <br /><br /><br />
 region for similar sales under similar conditions.                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 21.6.3 The formula on which the prices shall be based and determined pursuant to                              <br /><br /><br />
 Articles 21.6.2 (b) or (c) shall be approved by the Government prior to approval of                           <br /><br /><br />

23.1 In the conduct of Petroleum Operations, the Contractor shall:                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(a)    give preference to the purchase and use of goods manufactured, produced or                                      <br /><br /><br />
supplied in India provided that such goods are available on terms equal to or better                                   <br /><br /><br />
than imported goods with respect , to timing of delivery, quality and quantity                                         <br /><br /><br />
, required, price and other terms;                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(b)    employ Indian Subcontractors having the required skills or expertise, to the                                    <br /><br /><br />
maximum extent possible, insofar as their services are available on comparable                                         <br /><br /><br />
standards with those obtained elsewhere and at competitive prices and on                                               <br /><br /><br />
competitive terms; provided that where no such Subcontractors are available,                                           <br /><br /><br />
preference shall be given to non-Indian Subcontractors who utilize Indian goods to                                     <br /><br /><br />
the maximum extent possible subject however to the proviso in paragraph (a) above;                                     <br /><br /><br />
(c)    co-operate with domestic companies in India to enable them to develop skills and                                <br /><br /><br />
technology to service the petroleum industry;                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(d)    ensure that provisions in terms of paragraphs (a) to (c) above are contained in                                 <br /><br /><br />
contracts between the Operators and its Subcontractors.                                                                <br /><br /><br />
23.2    The Contractor shall establish appropriate procedures, including tender procedures, for                        <br /><br /><br />
the acquisition of goods and services which shall ensure that suppliers and Subcontractors                             <br /><br /><br />
in India are given adequate opportunity to compete for the supply of goods and services.                               <br /><br /><br />
The tender procedures shall include inter alia, the financial amounts or value of contracts                            <br /><br /><br />
which will be awarded on the basis of selective bidding or open competitive bidding, the                               <br /><br /><br />
procedures for such bidding and the exceptions to bidding in cases of emergency, and shall                             <br /><br /><br />
be subject to the approval of the Management Committee. The tender procedure is                                        <br /><br /><br />
attached as Appendix F which shall form part of this Contract.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 23.3    Within one hundred and twenty (120) days after the end of each Calendar Year, the                             <br /><br /><br />
 Contractor shall provide the Government with a report outlining its acliievements in                                  <br /><br /><br />
 utilizing Indian resources during that Calendar Year.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
23.4    In this Article "goods'' means equipment, material and supplies.                                               <br /><br /><br />

 24.1 Insurance                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 24.L1 The Contractor shail, during the term of this Contract, obtain and renew, as and            <br /><br /><br />
 when necessary insurance coverage for and in relation to Petroleum Operations for                 <br /><br /><br />
 such amounts and against such risks as are customarily or prudently insured in the                <br /><br /><br />
 international petroleum industry in accordance with good petroleum industry                       <br /><br /><br />
 practices, and shall furnish to the Government certificates evidencing that such                  <br /><br /><br />
 coverage is in effect. Such insurance policies shall include the Government and the               <br /><br /><br />
 licensee as additional insured and shall waive subrogation against the Government                 <br /><br /><br />
 and the licensee. The said insurance shall, without prejudice to the generality of                <br /><br /><br />
 the foregoing, cover:                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    Loss or damage to all installations, equipment and other assets for so long as             <br /><br /><br />
 they are used in or in connection with Petroleum Operations ; provided,                           <br /><br /><br />
 however, that if for any reason the Contractor fails to insure any such                           <br /><br /><br />
 installation, equipment or assets, it shall replace any loss thereof or repair any                <br /><br /><br />
 damage caused thereto;                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    Loss, damage or injury caused by pollution in the course of or as a result of              <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum Operations;                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    Loss of property or damage or bodily injury suffered by any third party in the             <br /><br /><br />
 course of or as a result of Petroleum Operations for which the Company may                        <br /><br /><br />
 be liable;                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 (d)    Any claim for which the Government may be liable relating to the loss of                   <br /><br /><br />
 property or damage or bodily injury suffered by any rtiird party in the course                    <br /><br /><br />
 of or as a result of Petroleum Operations for which the Contractor is liable to                   <br /><br /><br />
 indemnify the Government, the Licensee or the State Government;                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (e)    The Contractor's and / or the Operator's liability to its employees engaged in             <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum Operations.                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 24.1.2 The Contractor shall require its Subcontractors to obtain and maintain insurance           <br /><br /><br />
 against the risks referred to in Article 24.1.1 relating mutatis mutandis to such                 <br /><br /><br />
 Subcontractors.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
