﻿                             ARTICLE - 21                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                 TITLE TO PETROLEUM, DATA AND ASSETS                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
27.1    The Government is the sole owner of Petroleum underlying the Contract Area and shall           <br /><br /><br />
remain the sole owner of Petroleum produced pursuant to the provisions of this Contract                <br /><br /><br />
except as regards that part of Crude Oil or Gas the title whereof has passed to the                    <br /><br /><br />
Contractor or any other person in accordance with the provisions of this Contract.                     <br /><br /><br />
27.2    Title to Crude.Oil and / or Gas to which Contractor is entitled under this Contract, and       <br /><br /><br />
title to Crude Oil and / or Gas sold to Government or its nominee by the Companies shall               <br /><br /><br />
pass to the relevant Party or, as the case may be, to Government or its nominee at the                 <br /><br /><br />
Delivery Point. Contractor shall be responsible for all costs and risks prior to the                   <br /><br /><br />
Delivery Point and each Party shall be responsible for all costs and risks associated with             <br /><br /><br />
such Party's sliare after the Delivery Point and where the Government or its nominee                   <br /><br /><br />
purchases all or some of the Companies* share of Crude Oil or Condensate in accordance                 <br /><br /><br />
with Article 18, Government or its nominee shall be responsible for all costs and risks in             <br /><br /><br />
respect of the amount purchased, after the Delivery Point.                                             <br /><br /><br />
27.3    Title to all Data specified in Article 26 shall be vested in the Licensee and the Contractor   <br /><br /><br />
shall have the right to use thereof as therein provided.                                               <br /><br /><br />
27.4    Assets purchased by the Contractor for use in Petroleum Operations shall be owned by the       <br /><br /><br />
Parties comprising Contractor in proportion to their Participating Interest provided that              <br /><br /><br />
the Licensee shall have the right to require vesting of foli title and ownership in it, free of        <br /><br /><br />
charge and encumbrances, of any or all assets, whether fixed or movable, acquired and                  <br /><br /><br />
owned by the Contractor for use in Petroleum Operations inside or outside the Contract                 <br /><br /><br />
Area, such right to be exercisable at the Licensee's option either on recovery of the costs            <br /><br /><br />
of the assets or upon expiry or earlier termination of the Contract.                                   <br /><br /><br />
27.5    Contractor shall be responsible for proper maintenance, insurance and safety of all assets     <br /><br /><br />
acquired for Petroleum Operations (whether before or after the Effective Date) and for                 <br /><br /><br />
keeping them in good repair, order and working condition at all times, and the costs                   <br /><br /><br />
thereof shall be recoverable as Contract Costs in accordance with Appendix C.                          <br /><br /><br />
27.6    So long as this Contract remains in force, the Contractor shall, free of any charge for the    <br /><br /><br />
purpose of carrying out Petroleum Operations hereunder, have the exclusive use and custody             <br /><br /><br />
of the assets which have become the property of the Licensee subject* however, to Article              <br /><br /><br />

                                                         ARTICLE - 28                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                    ASSIGNMENT OF INTEREST                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                   28.1 Subject to the terms of this Article and other terms of this Contract, any Party       <br /><br /><br />
                    comprising the Contractor may assign, or transfer a part or all of its Participating       <br /><br /><br />
 Interest, with the prior written consent of the Government, which consent shall not be                        <br /><br /><br />
 unreasonably withheld, provided that the Government is satisfied that:                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    the prospective assignee or transferee is comparable to the assignor in terms of                       <br /><br /><br />
 financial standing and technical competence and its capacity and ability to meet                              <br /><br /><br />
 its obligations hereunder, and is willing to provide an unconditional undertaking                             <br /><br /><br />
 to assume its Participating Interest • share of obligations and to provide a                                  <br /><br /><br />
 guarantee in respect thereof as provided in the Contract;                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    the prospective assignee or transferee is not a company incorporated in a country                      <br /><br /><br />
 with which the Government for policy reasons, has restricted trade or business;                               <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    the prospective assignor or transferor and assignee or transferee respectively are                     <br /><br /><br />
 willing to comply with any reasonable conditions of the Government as may be                                  <br /><br /><br />
 necessary in the circumstances with a view to-ensuring performance under the                                  <br /><br /><br />
 Contract; and                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 (d)    the assignment or transfer will not adversely affect the performance or obligations                    <br /><br /><br />
 under this Contract or be contrary to the interests of India;                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 (c) Government shall not withhold its consent where the assignment or transfer to                             <br /><br /><br />
 another party comprising Contractor is as a result or withdrawal provisions of the                            <br /><br /><br />
 agreement between the Parties comprising Contractor;                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 (f) Requirement of Operating Agreement have been satisfied. •                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
28.2 An application by a Company for consent to assign or transfer shall be accompanied                        <br /><br /><br />
                  by all relevant information concerning the proposed assignment or transfer including         <br /><br /><br />
                  detailed information on the proposed assignee or transferee and its shareholding and         <br /><br /><br />
                  corporate structure, as was earlier required from the Companies constituting the             <br /><br /><br />
                  Contractor, the terms of the proposed assignment or transfer and the unconditional           <br /><br /><br />
                  undertaking referred to in (a) above. The applicant shall also submit such information       <br /><br /><br />
                  relating to the prospective assignee or transferee of the assignment or transfer as the      <br /><br /><br />
                  Government may reasonably require to enable proper consideration and disposal of             <br /><br /><br />
﻿28.3    tfo assignment or transfer shad be effective until the approval of the Government is                     <br /><br /><br />
received, which approval may be given by the Government on such terms as it may                                  <br /><br /><br />
deem fit. Upon assignment or transfer of its interest in this Contract, the assignor or                          <br /><br /><br />
transferor shall be released and discharged from its obligations hereunder only to. the                          <br /><br /><br />
extent that such obligations are assumed by the assignee or transferee with the                                  <br /><br /><br />
approval of the Government.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
28.4    Upon prior-notice to the Companies, a Government company may assign or transfer all or                   <br /><br /><br />
any part of its rights and interest under this Contract to any other Government company,                         <br /><br /><br />
authorized by the Government to explore for and exploit petroleum in the Contract Area. .                        <br /><br /><br />
28.5    An assignment' or transfer shall not be made so as to reduce the Participating Interest of a             <br /><br /><br />
constituent of the Contractor, at any time, to less than ten percent (10%) of the total                          <br /><br /><br />
Participating Interest of all the constituents of the Contractor, except, where the                              <br /><br /><br />
Government, on the recommendations of the Management Committee may, in special                                   <br /><br /><br />
circumstances, so permit.                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
28.6    Nothing contained in this Article 28 shall prevent a party comprising Contractor from                    <br /><br /><br />
mortgaging, pledging, charging or otherwise encumbering all or part of its Participating                         <br /><br /><br />
Interest for the purposes of security relating to finance required for performing the                            <br /><br /><br />
Contract, provided that:                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
(i)    such Party shall remain liable for all obligations relating to its Participating Interest;                <br /><br /><br />
(ii)    the encumbrance shall be expressly subordinated to the rights of the other Parties                       <br /><br /><br />
under this Contract;                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(iii)    such Party has given reasonable notice of such encumbrance and furnishes to all                         <br /><br /><br />
other Parties (including, for the avoidance of doubt, the Government) a certified                                <br /><br /><br />
copy of the executed instrument or instruments evidencing the encumbrance; and                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (iv)    prior consent of the Government shall be required (which consent shall not be                           <br /><br /><br />
                   unreasonably withheld) in connection with the hypothecation to any; lender with               <br /><br /><br />
                   international sensitivities for the Government.                                               <br /><br /><br />

estimated expenditure in respect of the-Work Program undertaken by the Contractor in the                                                 <br /><br /><br />

29.3 The guarantee shall provide:                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(a)    that the amount referred to in Article 29.2 shall be proportionately reduced at the end of                                        <br /><br /><br />
each Contract Year by the percentage which the actual expenditure bears to the total                                                     <br /><br /><br />
estimated expenditure for each phase of the Exploration Period, on presentation to the                                                   <br /><br /><br />
bank of a certificate signed by the Licensee tltat the said amount has been expended and                                                 <br /><br /><br />
that the said Guarantee may be reduced in accordance with its terms; and                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(b)    that, at the end of the phase, the guarantee will be released in favour of the Company                                            <br /><br /><br />
on presentation to die bank of a certificate from the Licensee that the obligation of                                                    <br /><br /><br />
the Contractor has been fulfilled and the guarantee may be released.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />

                               Exploration Period, a bank guarantee for the succeeding phase in terms of Articles 29.1                   <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                            ARTICLE 30                                                                 <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                       30.1 Without prejudice to the provisions of Article 30.6 or any other provisions of-this        <br /><br /><br />
Contract, Companies have the right to terminate this Contract:                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
(a)    with respect to any part of the Contract Area other than a Development Area then                                                <br /><br /><br />
producing, or that prior thereto had produced Petroleum, upon giving ninety (90)                                                       <br /><br /><br />
days 'written notice of its intention to do so; and                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(b)    with respect to any Development Area in which Petroleum Is being produced, or that                                              <br /><br /><br />
prior thereto had produced Petroleum, upon giving at least one hundred and eighty                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(180) days written notice of its intention to do so.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                        30.2 This Contract may, subject to the provisions hereinbelow and Article 31, be terminated by                 <br /><br /><br />
                           the Government upon giving ninety (90) days written notice of its intention to do so in the                 <br /><br /><br />
following circumstances, namely, that a Company:                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(a)    has knowingly submitted any false statement to the Government in any manner                                                     <br /><br /><br />
which was a material consideration in the execution of this Contract; or                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(b)    has intentionally and knowingly extracted or authorized the extraction of any mineral                                           <br /><br /><br />
not authorized to be extracted by the Contract or without the authority of the                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Government except such extractions as may be unavoidable as a result of operations                                                     <br /><br /><br />
conducted hereunder in accordance with generally accepted international petroleum                                                      <br /><br /><br />
industry practice which, when so extracted, were immediately notified to the                                                           <br /><br /><br />
Government and to the Licensee; or                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(c)    is adjudged bankrupt by a competent court or enters into any agreement or scheme of                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
composition with its creditors or takes advantage of any law for the benefit of debtors; or                                            <br /><br /><br />
(d)    has passed a resolution to apply to a competent court for liquidation of the Company                                            <br /><br /><br />
unless the liquidation is for the purpose of amalgamation or reconstruction of which the                                               <br /><br /><br />
Government has been given notice and the Government is satisfied that the Company's                                                    <br /><br /><br />
performance under this Contract would not be adversely affected thereby and has given                                                  <br /><br /><br />
its approval thereto; or                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(c) has assigned any interest in the Contract without the prior consent of the                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Government as provided in Article 28; or                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 <0                           fails to make any monetary payment required by law or under this Contract by the                         <br /><br /><br />
                              due date op,within the specified period after the due date; or                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿(g)    fails to comply with or contravenes the provisions of this Contract in a material                  <br /><br /><br />
• particular; or                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(h)    fails to comply with any final determination or award made by a sole expert or                     <br /><br /><br />
arbitrators pursuant to Article 33; or                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(i)    on notice of cancellation asprovided in Article 29.5.                                              <br /><br /><br />
PROVIDED THAT                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
Where the Contractor comprises two or more Companies, the Government shall not                            <br /><br /><br />
exercise its rights of termination pursuant to Article 30.2, on the occurrence, in relation to            <br /><br /><br />
one or more, but not all, of the Companies, of an event entitling the Government to                       <br /><br /><br />
terminate the Contract, if any other Company or Companies constituting the Contraptor                     <br /><br /><br />
satisfies the Government that it, or they, is/are willing and would be able to carry out the              <br /><br /><br />
obligations of the Contractor.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
30.3    This Contract may also be terminated by the Government on giving the requisite notice             <br /><br /><br />
specified above if the events specified in Article 30.2 (c) and (d) occur with respect to -a              <br /><br /><br />
Company which has given a guarantee pursuant to Article 29 subject, however, to Article 30.4.             <br /><br /><br />
30.4    If the circumstance or circumstances that give rise to the right of termination under Article     <br /><br /><br />
30.2 (f) or (g) or Article 30.3 are remedied by the Contractor within the ninety (90) day                 <br /><br /><br />
period or such extended period as may be granted by the government, following the notice                  <br /><br /><br />
of the Government's intention to terminate the Contract as aforesaid, such termination                    <br /><br /><br />
shall not become effective.                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
30.5    If the circumstance or circumstances that would otherwise result in termination are the           <br /><br /><br />
subject matter of proceedings under Article 33, then termination shall not take place so ■                <br /><br /><br />
long as such proceedings continue and thereafter may only take place when and if                          <br /><br /><br />
consistent with the arbitral award.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
30.6    On termination of this Contract, for any reason whatsoever, the rights and obligations of         <br /><br /><br />
the Contractor shall cease but such termination shall not affect any rights of any Party                  <br /><br /><br />
which may have accrued or any obligations undertaken, or incurred, pursuant to this                       <br /><br /><br />
Contract, by the Contractor or .any Party comprising the Contractor and not discharged by                 <br /><br /><br />
the Contractor or the Party prior to the date of termination.                                             <br /><br /><br />
30.7    In the event of termination pursuant to Article 30.1,30.2 or 30.3:                                <br /><br /><br />
 (a) the Government may require the Contractor for a period not exceeding one hundred                     <br /><br /><br />
 and eighty (180) days from the date of termination, to continue, for the account and                     <br /><br /><br />
 at the cost of the Government, Crude Oil or Natural Gas production activities until                      <br /><br /><br />
              the right to continue sucjuproduction has been transferred to another entity;               <br /><br /><br />
﻿ (b) in case of a Foreign Company, which is constituent of the Contractor, shall, subject         <br /><br /><br />
 to th$ provisions hereof have the right to remove and export all its property which              <br /><br /><br />
 has riot vested in the Licensee provided that in the event that ownership, of any                <br /><br /><br />
 property is in doubt, or disputed, such property shall.not be exported unless and                <br /><br /><br />
 until the doubt or dispute has been settled in favour of the Foreign Company.                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
30.8 Within ninety (90) days after the termination of this Contract pursuant to Article 30.1 or   <br /><br /><br />
30.2 or 30.3; or such longer period as the Government may agree, the Contractor shall             <br /><br /><br />
comply with Article J2.9 and any reasonably necessary action as directed by the                   <br /><br /><br />
Government to avoid Environmental Damage or hazards to human life or to the property              <br /><br /><br />
of others.                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                              ARTICLE - 31                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                             FORCE MAJEURE                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
31.1    Any non-performance or delay in performance by any Party hereto of any of its                                  <br /><br /><br />
obligations under this Contract, or in fulfilling any condition of any license or lease                                <br /><br /><br />
granted to such Party, or in meeting any requirement of the Act, the Rules or. any                                     <br /><br /><br />
license or lease issued thereunder, shall, except for the payment of monies due under                                  <br /><br /><br />
this Contract or under the Act and the Rules or any law, be excused if, and to die                                     <br /><br /><br />
extent that, such non-performance or delay in performance is caused by Force                                           <br /><br /><br />
Majeure as defined in this Article.                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
31.2    For the purpose of this Contract, the term Force Majeure means any cause or event, other                       <br /><br /><br />
than the unavailability of funds, whether similar to or different from those enumerated                                <br /><br /><br />
herein, lying beyond the reasonable control of, and unanticipated or unforeseeable by, and                             <br /><br /><br />
not brought about at the instance of, the Party claiming to be affected by such event, or                              <br /><br /><br />
which, if anticipated or foreseeable, could not be avoided or provided for, and which has                              <br /><br /><br />
caused the non-performance or delay in performance. Without limitation to the generality                               <br /><br /><br />
of the foregoing, the term Force Majeure shall include natural phenomena or calamities,                                <br /><br /><br />
earthquakes, typhoons, fires, wars declared or undeclared, hostilities, invasions, blockades,                          <br /><br /><br />
riots, insurrection and civil disturbances.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
31,3 Where a Party is claiming suspension of its obligations on account of Force Majeure,                              <br /><br /><br />
it shall promptly, but in no case later than seven (7) days after the occurrence of the                                <br /><br /><br />
event of Force Majeure, notify the other Parties in writing giving full particulars of the                             <br /><br /><br />
Force Majeure, the estimated duration thereof, the obligations affected and the                                        <br /><br /><br />
- reasons for its suspension.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
31.4 A Party claiming Forge Majeure shall exercise reasonable diligence to seek to                                     <br /><br /><br />
overcome the Force Majeure event and to mitigate the effects thereof on the                                            <br /><br /><br />
performance of its obligations under this Contract provided, however, that the                                         <br /><br /><br />
settlement of strikes or differences with employees shall be within the discretion of the                              <br /><br /><br />
Party having the difficulty. The Party affected shall promptly notify the other Parties                                <br /><br /><br />
as soon as the Force Majeure event has been removed and no longer prevents it from                                     <br /><br /><br />
complying with the obligations which have been suspended and shall thereafter resume                                   <br /><br /><br />
compliance with such obligations as soon as possible.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
31.5 The Party asserting the claim of Force Majeure shall have the burden of proving that                              <br /><br /><br />
the circumstances constitute valid grounds of Force Majeure under this Article and                                     <br /><br /><br />
• that such Party has exercised reasonable diligence and efforts to remedy the cause of                                <br /><br /><br />
any alleged Forpe Majeure.                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 <%T\J                                                      (                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
﻿31.5 Where a Party is prevented from exercising any rights or performing any obligations                                    <br /><br /><br />
. under this Contract due to Force Majeure, the time for the performance of the obligations                                 <br /><br /><br />
affected thereby and for performance of any obligation or the exercise of any right                                         <br /><br /><br />
dependent thereon, and the'term of any phase of the Exploration Period or this Contract,                                    <br /><br /><br />
may be extended by such additional period as may be agreed between the Parties or failing                                   <br /><br /><br />
agreeing by a sole expert in accordance with Article 33.                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
31.7                           Notwithstanding anything contained hereinabove, if aa event of Force Majeure occurs          <br /><br /><br />
                               and is likely to continue for a period in excess of thirty days, the Parties shall meet to   <br /><br /><br />
                               discuss the consequences of the Force Majeure and the course of action to be taken to        <br /><br /><br />
                               mitigate the effects thereof or to be adopted in the circumstances.                          <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                            ARTICLE -33                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                          SOLE EXPERT. CONCILIATION AND ARBITRATION                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
33.1    The Parties shad use their best efforts to settle amicably all disputes, differences or                               <br /><br /><br />
claims arising out of or in connection with any of the terms and conditions of this                                           <br /><br /><br />
Contract or concerning the interpretation or performance thereof.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
33.2    Except for matters which, by the terms of this Contract, the Parties have agreed to                                   <br /><br /><br />
refer to a sole expert and any other matters which the Parties may agree to so refer,                                         <br /><br /><br />
any dispute, difference or claim arising between the Parties hereunder which cannot be                                        <br /><br /><br />
settled amicably may, subject to Article 33.11, be submitted by any Party to                                                  <br /><br /><br />
arbitration pursuant to Article 33.3. Such sole expert shall be.an independent and                                            <br /><br /><br />
impartial person of international standing with relevant qualifications and experience                                        <br /><br /><br />
appointed by agreement between the Parties. Any sole expert appointed shall be                                                <br /><br /><br />
acting as an expert and not as an arbitrator and the decision of the sole expert on.                                          <br /><br /><br />
matters referred to him shall be final and binding on the Parties and not subject to                                          <br /><br /><br />
arbitration. If the Parties are unable to agree on a sole expert, and/or there is no                                          <br /><br /><br />
specific agreement with regard to matters to be referred to the sole expert, the matter                                       <br /><br /><br />
may be referred to arbitration.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
The parties further agree that the appointment of sole expert would be primarily for                                          <br /><br /><br />
the purpose of deciding matters which are technical in nature and require immediate                                           <br /><br /><br />
decision, more particular for the reasons that such decision not only have direct                                             <br /><br /><br />
bearing on day-to-day operation of the project, but failure to resolve within a time                                          <br /><br /><br />
bound period may result in the project implementation being delayed/prejudicially                                             <br /><br /><br />
effected.                                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
33.3    Subject to the provisions herein, the Parties hereby agree that any unresolved dispute,                               <br /><br /><br />
difference or claim which cannot be settled amicably within a reasonable time may,                                            <br /><br /><br />
except for those referred to in Article 33.2, be submitted to an arbitral tribunal for                                        <br /><br /><br />
final decision as hereinafter provided.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
33.4    The arbitral tribunal shall consist of three arbitrators. The Party or Parties instituting                            <br /><br /><br />
the arbitration shall appoint one arbitrator and the Party or Parties responding shall                                        <br /><br /><br />
appoint another arbitrator and both Parties shall so advise the other Parties. The two                                        <br /><br /><br />
arbitrators appointed by the Parties shall appoint the third arbitrator who shall act as                                      <br /><br /><br />
presiding Arbitrator.                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                              ‘imi-                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿ 33.5         Any Party may, after appointing an arbitrator, request the other Party(ies) in writing      <br /><br /><br />
           to appoint the second arbitrator. If such other Party fails to appoint an arbitrator           <br /><br /><br />
           within thirty(30) days of receipt of the written request to do so, such arbitrator may,        <br /><br /><br />
           at the request of the first Party, be appointed by the Chief Justice of India or any           <br /><br /><br />
           person or institution designated'by him within sixty(60) days of the receipt of such           <br /><br /><br />
           request in case of an international commercial arbitration as defined in the Arbitration       <br /><br /><br />
           aud Conciliation Act, 1996 and where Parties to the arbitration comprised of only the          <br /><br /><br />
           domestic compames/bodies, the appointment of the arbitrator referred in this sub¬              <br /><br /><br />
           article shall, be done by the Chief Justice of the High Court having jurisdiction or any       <br /><br /><br />
           person or institution designated by him within sixty(60) days of the receipt of such           <br /><br /><br />
           request.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
33.6 If the two arbitrators appointed by the Parties fail to agree on appointment of the                  <br /><br /><br />
third arbitrator within thirty(30) days of the appointment of the second arbitrator and                   <br /><br /><br />
if the Parties do not otherwise agree, the Chief Justice of India or any person or                        <br /><br /><br />
institution designated by him in case of an international commercial arbitration and                      <br /><br /><br />
Chief Justice of the High Court having jurisdiction or any person or institution                          <br /><br /><br />
designated by him in case of an arbitration involving only domestic companies, at the                     <br /><br /><br />
request of either Party and in consultation with both, appoint the third arbitrator                       <br /><br /><br />
keeping in view that he is not a national of the country of any of the Parties to the                     <br /><br /><br />
arbitration proceedings where the Parties to the dispute belong to different                              <br /><br /><br />
nationalities.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
33.7    If any of the arbitrators fails or is.unable to act, his successor shall be appointed in the      <br /><br /><br />
manner set out in this Article as if he was the first appointment.                                        <br /><br /><br />
33.8    The decision of the arbitral tribunal, and, in the case of difference among the                   <br /><br /><br />
arbitrators, the decision of the majority, shall be final and binding upon the Parties.                   <br /><br /><br />
33.9    Arbitration proceedings shall be conducted in accordance with the Arbitration and                 <br /><br /><br />
Conciliation Act 1996 except that in the event of any conflict between this Act and                       <br /><br /><br />
the provisions of this Article 33, the provisions of the Act shall apply.                                 <br /><br /><br />
33.10    The right to arbitrate disputes and claims under this Contract shall survive the                 <br /><br /><br />
termination of this Contract.                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
33.11    Prior to submitting a dispute to arbitration, a party may submit the matter for                  <br /><br /><br />
conciliation under the Indian Arbitration and Conciliation Act 1996 as amended or re¬                     <br /><br /><br />
enacted from time to time by a sole conciliator to be appointed by mutual agreement                       <br /><br /><br />
of the Parties. If the Parties fail to agree on a conciliator in accordance with the said                 <br /><br /><br />
rules, the matter may be submitted for arbitration. No arbitration proceedings shall be                   <br /><br /><br />
instituted while conciliation proceedings are pending.                                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿ f                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
33.12 The venue of conciliation or arbitration proceedings pursuant to this Article, unless     <br /><br /><br />
t^e Parties otherwise agree, shall be in New Delhi and shall be conducted in the                <br /><br /><br />
English language. Insofar as practicable, the Parties shall continue to implement the           <br /><br /><br />
terms of this Contract notwithstanding the initiation of arbitral proceedings and any.          <br /><br /><br />
pending claim or dispute.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
33.13 The fees and expenses of a sole expert or conciliator appointed by the Parties shall be   <br /><br /><br />
' borne equally by the Parties. Unless otherwise agreed to by the parties, assessment of        <br /><br /><br />
the costs qf arbitration including incidental expenses and liability for the payment            <br /><br /><br />
thereof shall be at the discretion of the arbitrators.    ^                                     <br /><br /><br />

 Insurance premium and costs incurred for insurance pursuant to Article 24 of the                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 Contract, provided that such insurance is customary, affords prudent protection against                                              <br /><br /><br />

 insurance Companies which are not Affiliates. Except as provided in Sections 3.2 (ix),                                               <br /><br /><br />
 Section 3.2(x) and Section 3.2(xi), actual costs and losses incurred shall be allowable to                                           <br /><br /><br />
 the extent not made good by insurance. Sucii costs may include, but are not limited to,                                              <br /><br /><br />
 repair and replacement of property in the Contract Area resulting from damages or                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 losses incurred by fife, flood, storm, theft, accident or such other cause.                                                          <br /><br /><br />

 defending or prosecuting lawsuits involving the Contract Area or any third party                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 claim arising' out of Petroleum. Operations under the Contract, or sums paid in                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 respect of legal services necessary for the protection of the joint interest of                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 Government and the Contractor, shall be allowable. Such expenditures shall                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 include attorney’s fee, court costs, of investigation and procurement of evidence                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 and amounts paid in settlement or satisfaction of any such litigation and claims                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 providing such costs are not covered elsewhere in the Accounting Procedure. Where                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 legal services are rendered in such matters by Contractor or an Affiliate, such                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 compensation shall be included instead under Section 3.1.2. or 3.1.4 (ii) above as .                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 applicable.                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

3.4    Incidental Income and Credits                                                             <br /><br /><br />
All incidental income and proceeds received from Petroleum Operations under the Contract,        <br /><br /><br />
including but not limited to the items listed below, shall be credited to the accounts under the <br /><br /><br />
Contract and shall be taken into account for cost recovery, production sharing and participation <br /><br /><br />
purposes in the manner described in Articles 13,14 and 15 of the Contract                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿ (i)    The proceeds of any insurance or claim or judicial awards in connection with                             <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum Operations under the Contract or any assets charged to the accounts                                   <br /><br /><br />
 under the Contract where such operations or assets have been insured and the                                    <br /><br /><br />
 premia charged to the accounts under the Contract.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 (ii)    Revenue received from third parties for the use of property or assets, the cost of                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 which has been cliarged to the accounts under the Contract;                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (iii)    Any adjustment received by the Contractor from the suppliers/roanufacturers or their                   <br /><br /><br />
 agents in connection with defective material, the cost of which was previously                                  <br /><br /><br />
 charged by the Contractor to the accounts under the Contract.                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (iv)    Rentals, refunds or other credits received by the Contractor which apply to any                         <br /><br /><br />
 charge wiuch has been made to the accounts under the Contract;                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 (v)    Prices originally cliarged to the accounts under the Contract for materials                              <br /><br /><br />
 subsequently exported from the Republic of India without being used in Petroleum                                <br /><br /><br />
 Operations under the Contract;                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 (vi)    Proceeds from the sale or exchange by the Contractor of plant or facilities from a                      <br /><br /><br />
 Field, the acquisition costs of wliich have been charged to the accounts under the                              <br /><br /><br />
 Contract for the relevant Field;                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 (vii)    Proceeds from the sale or exchange by the Contractor of any Petroleum rights, being                    <br /><br /><br />
 an interest in the Contract Area;                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 (viii) Legal costs charged to the accounts under Section 3.1.11 of this Accounting                              <br /><br /><br />
 Procedure and subsequently recovered by the Contractor.                                                         <br /><br /><br />

                                                     RECORDS AND INVENTORIES OF ASSETS                                                        <br /><br /><br />

 4.1 Records                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 4.1.1    The Contractor shall keep and maintain detailed records of property and assets in                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 use for or in connection with Petroleum Operations under the Contract in                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 accordance with normal practices in exploration and production.activities of the                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 international petroleum' industry. Such records shall include information on                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 quantities, location and condition of such property and assets, and whether such                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 property, or assets are leased or owned.                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 4.1.2    The Contractor shall furnish particulars to the Government, by notice in writing as                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 provided in the Contract, at six monthly intervals of all assets acquired by the                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 Contractor to be used or in connection with Petroleum Operations during the.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 period Immediately preceding the delivery of such notice.                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
4.2 Inventories                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
4.2.1    The Contractor shall'                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
a)    not less than once every twelve (12) Months with respect to moveable assets;                                                            <br /><br /><br />
and                                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
b)    not less than once every three (3) Years with respect to immovable assets,                                                              <br /><br /><br />
take an inventory of the assets used for or in connection with Petroleum                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
Operations in terms of the Contract and address and deliver such inventory to                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
the Government together with a written statement of the principles upon which                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
valuation of the assets mentioned in such inventory has been based.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
4.2.2    The Contractor shall give the Government at least thirty (30) days notice in writing                                                 <br /><br /><br />
in the manner provided for in the Contract of its intention to take the inventory                                                             <br /><br /><br />
referred to in Section 4.2.1 and the Government shall have the right to be                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
represented when such inventory is taken.                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
4.2.3    When an assignment of rights under the Contract takes place, a special inventory                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
shall be taken by the Contractor at the request of the assignee provided that the                                                             <br /><br /><br />
cost of such inventory is borne by the assignee and paid to the Contractor.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />

 carrying on drilling and production operations and pumping to Field storage, as                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 well as quantities re-injected.                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 5.1.5 The quantities of Crude Oil, Condensate and Natural Gas unavoidably lost.                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 5.1.7    The quantities of Natural Gas flared and vented.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />

 Field.                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />

 natural Condensate..                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />

 question.                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                          APPENDIX D                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                      CALCULATION OF THE                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                 INVESTMENT MULTIPLE FOR PRODUCTION SHARING PURPOSES                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.    In accordance with the provisions of Article 15, the share of the Government and the                                    <br /><br /><br />
Contractor respectively of Profit Petroleum from any Field in any Year shall be determined                                    <br /><br /><br />
by the Investment . Multiple earned by the Companies from the Field at the end of the                                         <br /><br /><br />
preceding Year. These measures of profitability shall be calculated on the basis of the                                       <br /><br /><br />
appropriate net cash flows as specified in this Appendix D.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
Investment Multiple                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
2.    The "Net Cash Income" of the Companies from the Field in any particular Year is the                                     <br /><br /><br />
aggregate value for the Year of the following:                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(*) Cost Petroleum entitlement of the Companies as provided in Article 14;                                                    <br /><br /><br />
plus                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(ii)    Profit Petroleum entitlement of the Companies as provided in Article 15;                                              <br /><br /><br />
plus                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(iii)    the Companies's share of all incidental income (of the type specified in section                                     <br /><br /><br />
3.4 of the Accounting Procedure) arising from Petroleum Operations;                                                           <br /><br /><br />
less                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(iv)    the Compantes's share of all Production Costs incurred on or in the Field;                                            <br /><br /><br />
less                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(v)    the notional income tax, determined in accordance with paragraph 7 of this                                             <br /><br /><br />
Appendix, payable by the Companies on profits and gains from the Field.                                                       <br /><br /><br />
3. The "Investment" made by the Companies in the Field in any particular Year is the                                          <br /><br /><br />
aggregate value for the Year of :                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                           I) the Companies’s share of Exploration Costs incurred in the Contract Area and                    <br /><br /><br />
                           apportioned to the Field in the same proportion that such Costs were recovered                     <br /><br /><br />
                           pursuant to Article 14.4;.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                           plus                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                           ii) The Companies's share of Development Costs incurred in the Field.                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
4,                         For the purpose of the calculation of the Investment Multiple, costs or expenditures               <br /><br /><br />
                           which are not allowable as provided in the Accounting Procedure shall be excluded                  <br /><br /><br />
                           from ContractCosts and be disregarded.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                     a-.                                   <// \ V 7                                          <br /><br /><br />
﻿5.    The Investment Multiple ratio earned by the Companies as at the end of any Year         <br /><br /><br />
ftorir the Field shall b.e calculated by dividing the aggregate value of the addition of      <br /><br /><br />
each of the annual Net Cash Incomes (accumulated, without interest, up to and                 <br /><br /><br />
including that Year starting from the Year in which Production Costs were first               <br /><br /><br />
incurred or Production first arose on or in the Field) by the aggregate value of the          <br /><br /><br />
addition of each of the annual Investments (accumulated, without interest, up to and          <br /><br /><br />
including that Year starting from the Year in which Exploration and Development               <br /><br /><br />
Costs were first incurred).                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
6.    Profit Petroleum from the Field in any Year shall be shared between the Government      <br /><br /><br />
and the Contractor in accordance with the value of the Investment Multiple earned by          <br /><br /><br />
the Companies as at the end of the previous Year pursuant to Articles 15.2 -15.7.             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
General                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
7. The applicable cash flows set out in paragraphs 2 and 3 of this Appendix shall be          <br /><br /><br />
separately identified and calculated in respect, of each Field.                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
8.  In determining the amount of notional income tax to be deducted in the applicable         <br /><br /><br />
    cash flows specified in paragraph 2 of this Appendix, a notional income tax liability in  <br /><br /><br />
    respect of the Field shall be determined for .each Company comprising the Contractor,     <br /><br /><br />
    as if the conduct of Petroleum Operations by the Company in the Field constituted the     <br /><br /><br />
    sole business of the Company and as if the provisions of the Income-Tax Act, 1961,        <br /><br /><br />
    with respect to the computation of income tax on the basis of the income and              <br /><br /><br />
    deductions provided for in Article 16 of this Contract were accordingly applicable        <br /><br /><br />
    separately to the Field, disregarding any income, allowances, deductions, losses or       <br /><br /><br />
    set-off of losses from any other contract Area or business of the Company.                <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                 APPENDIX F                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                 PROCEDURE FOR ACQUISITION OF GOODS AND SERVICES                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 L OBJECTIVES                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 The objectives of these procedures are to:                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    ensure the goods and services acquired by the Operator for the carrying out of the                            <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum Operations are acquired at the optimum cost taking into consideration all                                  <br /><br /><br />
 relevant factors including price, quality, delivery times and the reliability of potential •                         <br /><br /><br />
 suppliers,                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    ensure that goods and services are. delivered in a timely manner taking into                                  <br /><br /><br />
 consideration the consequences of delays in the acquisition of these goods and                                       <br /><br /><br />
 services on the project as a whole.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    ensure that the provisions of Article 23 of the Contract are implemented.                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
H    PRINCIPLES                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
The principles upon which these procedures are based are:                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(a)    The parties must be satisfied that the Operator is working to an agreed procedure for                          <br /><br /><br />
acquiring goods and services which is auditable and in accordance with the provisions                                 <br /><br /><br />
of the Contract.                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(b)    The Operator must have the ability to acquire goods and services expeditiously so                              <br /><br /><br />
that the project schedules in respect of Approved Work Programmes are maintained.                                     <br /><br /><br />
m    procedures                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
The procedures to be adopted, by the Operator for the acquisition of goods and services                               <br /><br /><br />
shall be as follows:                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                          Procedure A     Procedure B                         Procedure C             <br /><br /><br />
            Applicable to Exploration,    $ 25,000 to             $ 100,001 to                more than $             <br /><br /><br />
            Appraisal, Development and    $ 100,000                 $ 300,000                   300,000               <br /><br /><br />
            Production Operations                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                          ✓                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                          /,                                                                     ^3^                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                               Li     / •->     L.                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                 For Contracts valued at less than USS 25.Q0Q                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                 Tile Operator will be at liberty to determine the preferred method of acquiring goods and services      <br /><br /><br />
                                 valued at less than USS 25,000 with the understanding that at least three (3) quotations from           <br /><br /><br />
                                 selected suppliers (including at least one (1) Indian supplier) will be obtained. For items valued at   <br /><br /><br />
                                 greater than USS 10,000, Operator is required to report to the Operating Committee if the quote         <br /><br /><br />
                                 accepted exceeds the lowest quote by more than 20 percent. Operator will promptly report to the         <br /><br /><br />
                                 Operating Committee the Operator's reasons for not selecting the lowest quote.                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                 Procedure A:                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />

﻿VI Operator to contract a Agent, Audit Rights and Assigaability                                      <br /><br /><br />
(a)    The Operator shall act as an agent to the Parties in dealings with contractors and suppliers. <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Unless otherwise determined by the Management Committee, in negotiating contracts with        <br /><br /><br />
third parties in excess of US D 10,000, Operator shall procure the right to audit clause.            <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Unless otherwise approved by the Management Committee, the Operator shall ensure that         <br /><br /><br />
any contract awarded may be freely assigned to any successor of the Operator in the event            <br /><br /><br />
of resignation or removal of the Operator.                                                           <br /><br /><br />
VU In cases of emergency, Operator may award sub-contracts or acquire goods and services             <br /><br /><br />
without following the procedure set our above, provided such transactions are reported to            <br /><br /><br />
the Operating Committee at it’s first meeting following such award.                                  <br /><br /><br />
